## Chronological information

### Timeline

[3643 BBY](/wiki/3643_BBY "3643 BBY")[[18]](#cite_note-Time_Question-18)–3621 BBY[[19]](#cite_note-LOTS_date-19)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:VideoGame)

:   "*Even among its interactive peers, 'The Old Republic' is touted as a leap forward. Much as the first 'Star Wars' movie in 1977 changed history, its makers hope to create a new gold standard for gaming.*"
:   ―[*Los Angeles Times*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Los_Angeles_Times "wikipedia:Los Angeles Times")[[20]](#cite_note-LA_Times-20)

***Star Wars: The Old Republic***, simply known as ***SWTOR*** or ***TOR***, is a [massively multiplayer online roleplaying game](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Massively_multiplayer_online_role-playing_game "wikipedia:Massively multiplayer online role-playing game") (MMORPG) that was originally produced by [BioWare](/wiki/BioWare "BioWare"), a subsidiary of [Electronic Arts](/wiki/Electronic_Arts "Electronic Arts"), and published by [LucasArts](/wiki/LucasArts "LucasArts"). Developed over the course of more than five years by BioWare Austin and LucasArts at a cost of over $200 million, *Star Wars: The Old Republic* was first conceived in [2005](/wiki/2005 "2005") as an MMORPG follow-up to BioWare's previous [video games](/wiki/Star_Wars_video_games "Star Wars video games"), the popular *[Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Knights_of_the_Old_Republic "Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic")* and its sequel *[Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic II: The Sith Lords](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Knights_of_the_Old_Republic_II:_The_Sith_Lords "Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic II: The Sith Lords")*, and the game was first announced on [October 21](/wiki/October_21 "October 21"), [2008](/wiki/2008 "2008"). The game itself was released to the public on [December 20](/wiki/December_20 "December 20"), [2011](/wiki/2011 "2011"), and *The Old Republic* is accompanied by an expansive metaseries of *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* multimedia, including a four-book novel [series](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Old_Republic_(novel_series) "Star Wars: The Old Republic (novel series)"), three comic series ([*Threat of Peace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Old_Republic,_Threat_of_Peace "Star Wars: The Old Republic, Threat of Peace"), [*Blood of the Empire*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Old_Republic,_Blood_of_the_Empire "Star Wars: The Old Republic, Blood of the Empire"), and *[Star Wars: The Old Republic — The Lost Suns](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Old_Republic_%E2%80%94_The_Lost_Suns "Star Wars: The Old Republic — The Lost Suns")*), and a number of short stories, as well as additional content.

*Star Wars: The Old Republic* succeeded [Sony](/wiki/Sony "Sony")'s *[Star Wars Galaxies](/wiki/Star_Wars_Galaxies "Star Wars Galaxies")* as the main *Star Wars* MMORPG, and *Galaxies* went permanently offline shortly before *The Old Republic* was released in December 2011. Set over three hundred years after the events of the *Knights of the Old Republic* games, *The Old Republic* features seventeen fully explorable planets, eight unique classes divided into the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic/Legends "Galactic Republic/Legends") and [Sith Empire](/wiki/Sith_Empire_(Post%E2%80%93Great_Hyperspace_War) "Sith Empire (Post–Great Hyperspace War)") factions, and over 1,600 hours of story in addition to over a dozen group Flashpoints and Operations, and it is the first MMORPG to feature full-scale voice acting. The game features extensive references to pre-existing *Star Wars* continuity, and introduces thousands of new characters, locations, items, groups, and events to the *Star Wars* universe as it depicts the [conflict](/wiki/Galactic_War "Galactic War") between the Republic and the Empire. With the discarding of the [Expanded Universe](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends") on [April 25](/wiki/April_25 "April 25"), [2014](/wiki/2014 "2014"), *Star Wars: The Old Republic* is the only remaining source that continues to produce Legends information aside from the official [*Star Wars* Blog](/wiki/Star_Wars_Blog "Star Wars Blog").

Over one million subscribers registered in the first three days following *The Old Republic*'s release, and over a million had begun to play *The Old Republic* by [December 26](/wiki/December_26 "December 26"), making it the fastest-growing subscription MMORPG in history. *The Old Republic* has received generally positive reviews from critics, with a score of 85 on the review aggregation website [Metacritic](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Metacritic "wikipedia:Metacritic"), though it has received some criticism by players for the lack of late-game content, which has led the game's developers to focus on the addition of upper-level content in many of their updates. Due to declining subscription numbers during the summer of [2012](/wiki/2012 "2012"), *The Old Republic* introduced a Free-to-Play option in [November](/wiki/November "November") 2012, and the game's first digital expansion, [*Rise of the Hutt Cartel*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Old_Republic:_Rise_of_the_Hutt_Cartel "Star Wars: The Old Republic: Rise of the Hutt Cartel"), was released in [April](/wiki/April "April") [2013](/wiki/2013 "2013"). *The Old Republic* has received several dozens major content updates so far, and the second Digital Expansion, [*Galactic Starfighter*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Old_Republic:_Galactic_Starfighter "Star Wars: The Old Republic: Galactic Starfighter"), was released to free-to-play users in [February](/wiki/February "February") 2014. *Galactic Starfighter* was released to active subscribers on [December 3](/wiki/December_3 "December 3"), 2013, and was released to Preferred Status players on [January 14](/wiki/January_14 "January 14"). A third Digital Expansion, [*Galactic Strongholds*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Old_Republic:_Galactic_Strongholds "Star Wars: The Old Republic: Galactic Strongholds"), was released in [August](/wiki/August "August") 2014, and a fourth expansion, [*Shadow of Revan*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Old_Republic:_Shadow_of_Revan "Star Wars: The Old Republic: Shadow of Revan"), was released on [December 9](/wiki/December_9 "December 9"). With the next two digital expansions: [*Knights of the Fallen Empire*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Old_Republic:_Knights_of_the_Fallen_Empire "Star Wars: The Old Republic: Knights of the Fallen Empire") ([October 27](/wiki/October_27 "October 27"), [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015")), and [*Knights of the Eternal Throne*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Old_Republic:_Knights_of_the_Eternal_Throne "Star Wars: The Old Republic: Knights of the Eternal Throne") ([December 2](/wiki/December_2 "December 2"), [2016](/wiki/2016 "2016")), the game took a narrative twist, focusing on a new faction, the [Eternal Empire](/wiki/Eternal_Empire "Eternal Empire"). On [April 13](/wiki/April_13 "April 13"), [2019](/wiki/2019 "2019"), it was announced that a seventh expansion would be coming to the game, titled [*Onslaught*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Old_Republic:_Onslaught "Star Wars: The Old Republic: Onslaught"). *Onslaught* was released on [October 22](/wiki/October_22 "October 22"), 2019. In celebration for the tenth-year anniversary, an eighth expansion was announced on [July 1](/wiki/July_1 "July 1"), [2021](/wiki/2021 "2021"), titled [*Legacy of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Old_Republic:_Legacy_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: The Old Republic: Legacy of the Sith"). *Legacy of the Sith* was released on [February 15](/wiki/February_15 "February 15"), [2022](/wiki/2022 "2022").

In June [2023](/wiki/2023 "2023"), [BioWare](/wiki/BioWare "BioWare") handed off maintenance and development of *Star Wars: The Old Republic* to [Broadsword Online Games](/wiki/Broadsword_Online_Games "Broadsword Online Games"). The majority of the *Old Republic* development team at BioWare was intended to join Broadsword to continue to work on the game.[[2]](#cite_note-Gamespot-2)[[3]](#cite_note-Studio_Update-3) On [December 19](/wiki/December_19 "December 19"), [2025](/wiki/2025 "2025"), it was announced that the *Legacy of the Sith* storyline would end in Game Update 7.9 and that a ninth expansion would be released sometime in [2026](/wiki/2026 "2026") for the fifteen-year anniversary of the game.[[21]](#cite_note-Q4_2025-21)

## Opening crawl

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | THE SITH WARRIOR | | --- | | ``` The Sith Empire tightens its grip on the galaxy. The Galactic Republic and its Jedi defenders lie weakened and vulnerable after the Empire's successful military campaign.  With a fragile peace negotiated, the Empire sends all potential Sith to undergo cruel and deadly trials at its Academy on the harsh planet KORRIBAN.  Today, one of the Empire's most promising young warriors has been secretly summoned by an influential overseer to face the dark side trials much sooner than expected.... ``` | |  |  | THE IMPERIAL AGENT | | --- | | ``` It is a pivotal time for the Sith Empire. Having secured an uneasy truce with the Galactic Republic, the Empire now seeks allies among the neutral systems.  The foul planet HUTTA is the Empire's latest target, but its wealthy and corrupt crime lords refuse to take sides in the cold war between Republic and Empire.  To tip the scales, Imperial Intelligence's latest shadowy operative has been dispatched to Hutta under command of the Empire's mysterious spymaster.... ``` | |  |  | THE BOUNTY HUNTER | | --- | | ``` THE GREAT HUNT begins. While the Sith Empire and the Galactic Republic scheme against each other, a bloody contest rages in the frontier systems.  Mercenaries from across the galaxy compete for the privilege of entering a dangerous manhunt where the must capture or eliminate the most notorious and elusive targets.  In the polluted swamps of HUTTA, a tough young gunfighter teams with an aging bounty hunter to secure an invitation to this deadly struggle for fortune and glory.... ``` | |  |  | THE SITH INQUISITOR | | --- | | ``` The power of the dark side grows. The SITH EMPIRE has won a major victory against the Galactic Republic and its Jedi guardians, conquering and enslaving many new worlds.  With a fragile peace in place, the Empire sends its slaves to the ancient Sith stronghold of KORRIBAN, hoping to unearth relics of vast power that can be used to dominate the galaxy.  One slave, powerful with the Force, has been released from servitude and forced to master the dark arts of the Sith or die trying.... ``` | |  | |

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | THE SMUGGLER | | --- | | ``` Anarchy rules in the frontier systems. While the Galactic Republic struggles to recover from its conflict with the Sith Empire, reckless mercenaries profit from the interstellar turmoil.  ORD MANTELL, a world ravaged by civil war between pro-Republic citizens and separatist extremists, has become a lucrative destination for free traders.  Now, a daring captain-for-hire has come to deliver a cargo of weapons to the combat zone, flying a swift freighter through a deadly barrage of separatist attacks.... ``` | |  |  | THE JEDI KNIGHT | | --- | | ``` It is a dark era for the Jedi Order. The Sith Empire obliterated the Jedi Temple on Coruscant and slaughtered many of the Republic's brave defenders during the last war.  The surviving Jedi have withdrawn to their ancient homeworld of TYTHON, where they take advantage of a fragile peace to train a new generation of guardians for the galaxy.  Now a new hope emerges. A young Padawan strong in the Force journeys to Tython's dangerous wilderness to complete the final Jedi trials and become a Knight of the Republic.... ``` | |  |  | THE JEDI CONSULAR | | --- | | ``` Evil threatens to consume the galaxy. The Sith Empire's relentless assault destroyed the Jedi Temple and drove the Republic's defenders into exile during the last war.  A fragile peace has been negotiated, and the Jedi have returned to their long-abandoned homeworld of TYTHON to regroup and investigate their ancient origins."  Now, a wise young Padawan travels to Tython's mountain ruins on a perilous quest to complete the Jedi trials and master the mysteries of the Force.... ``` | |  |  | THE REPUBLIC TROOPER | | --- | | ``` Chaos grips the Galactic Republic. Influential star systems break away from the millennia-old alliance, angered over the Senate's treaty with the Sith Empire.  On the planet of ORD MANTELL, civil war erupts between loyal Republic citizens and violent separatist extremists waging a campaign of terror against their own people.  Now, an elite young sergeant from the Republic's famous HAVOC SQUAD has arrived to help defeat the separatists and restore peace to this war-ravaged world.... ``` | |  | |

| KNIGHTS OF THE FALLEN EMPIRE |
| --- |
| ``` It is a time of chaos. A mysterious army led by twin conquerors has carved a path of destruction across the worlds of the warring Galactic Republic and Sith Empire, then disappeared into uncharted space.  Meanwhile, an older threat still looms: the former SITH EMPEROR, revitalized after annihilating all life on the planet Ziost, has similarly vanished without a trace.  Determined to hunt down these dangerous foes at any cost, Imperial leader DARTH MARR gathers allies from both factions to join his incursion into the far reaches of Wild Space.... ``` |
|  |

| KNIGHTS OF THE ETERNAL THRONE |
| --- |
| ``` A new threat rises. In the wake of Emperor Arcann's defeat, his depraved sister Vaylin has seized control of the ETERNAL EMPIRE and begun spreading terror across known space.  The galaxy's only hope is the ALLIANCE: a bold resistance group that wages a daring campaign to overthrow Vaylin and end the tyranny of her Eternal Empire.  As the Alliance grows in strength, Vaylin sets out to dominate the galaxy with the fearsome might of the Eternal Throne. Her conquest begins with the peaceful world of Voss... ``` |
|  |

| ONSLAUGHT |
| --- |
| ``` War consumes the galaxy. Hungering for dominance, the ruthless SITH EMPIRE fights to destroy their ancient enemies in the GALACTIC REPUBLIC.  Assembling an overwhelming fleet of the Empire's most powerful warships, DARTH MALGUS sets out to obliterate a new and highly advanced Republic shipyard on the planet Corellia.  Now, desperate to prevent this catastrophe, the Republic rushes to gather the force necessary to defend this vital facility - one that could finally turn the tide of the war in their favor... ``` |
|  |

| LEGACY OF THE SITH (Republic) |
| --- |
| ``` The fate of the galaxy balances on a razor's edge. The Sith Empire and Galactic Republic - still consumed by the flames of war - viciously compete for any advantage that can secure victory.  No war can be won without KOLTO, a vital medical resource harvested by the unaligned and reclusive Selkath of Manaan - placing their ocean planet at the center of the conflict.  Plans are already in motion to ensure this precious substance flows only one way - towards the glory of the Empire. The Republic must act quickly of risk losing everything.... ``` |
|  |

| LEGACY OF THE SITH (Empire) |
| --- |
| ``` The fate of the galaxy balances on a razor's edge. The Sith Empire and Galactic Republic - still consumed by the flames of war - viciously compete for any advantage that can secure victory.  With vital resources in short supply, the Empire turns its gaze to Manaan, an ocean planet overflowing with the indispensable, but rare, medical substance known as KOLTO.  Manaan's reclusive people, the Selkath, control the flow of kolto with an uncharitable grasp. Determined to seize all kolto for themselves, the Empire's forces prepare for invasion.... ``` |
|  |

## Plot summary

### Prologue

:   "*Thus began the unprecedented stalemate. The Jedi reconnecting with their roots, the Republic nursing its wounds, the Sith consolidating their power in a galaxy divided between darkness and light.*"
:   ―Jedi Master Gnost-Dural — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a9/ColdWarStalemate.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250308173048)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:ColdWarStalemate.flac "File:ColdWarStalemate.flac"))[[22]](#cite_note-Timeline1-22)

 [![A rough map of the galactic borders during the Cold War](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/TreatyofCoruscantborders.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090704002337) [![A rough map of the galactic borders during the Cold War](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/TreatyofCoruscantborders.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20090704002337)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/TreatyofCoruscantborders.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090704002337) 

A rough map of the galactic borders during the Cold War

 

In [3681 BBY](/wiki/3681_BBY "3681 BBY"), a [reconstituted Sith Empire](/wiki/Sith_Empire_(Post%E2%80%93Great_Hyperspace_War) "Sith Empire (Post–Great Hyperspace War)"), the survivors of the [Old Sith Empire](/wiki/Sith_Empire/Legends "Sith Empire/Legends") that lost the [Great Hyperspace War](/wiki/Great_Hyperspace_War/Legends "Great Hyperspace War/Legends") over a thousand [years](/wiki/Standard_year/Legends "Standard year/Legends") earlier, return to [the larger galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy/Legends "The galaxy/Legends") under the leadership of an [immortal](/wiki/Immortality/Legends "Immortality/Legends") [Sith Emperor](/wiki/Tenebrae "Tenebrae") and invade the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic/Legends "Galactic Republic/Legends"), sparking the [Great Galactic War](/wiki/Great_Galactic_War "Great Galactic War"). Though the Empire achieved many victories in the early years of the conflict, the Republic eventually rallied and won several hard-earned victories, which caused the war to drag on for a total of twenty-eight years. Finally, in [3653 BBY](/wiki/3653_BBY "3653 BBY"), the Empire attacked the Republic [capital](/wiki/Capital/Legends "Capital/Legends") of [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant/Legends "Coruscant/Legends") in what became known as the [Sacking of Coruscant](/wiki/Sacking_of_Coruscant "Sacking of Coruscant") and forced the Republic to accept the [Treaty of Coruscant](/wiki/Treaty_of_Coruscant "Treaty of Coruscant"), ending the war and beginning a tense [Cold War](/wiki/Cold_War_(Galactic_Republic%E2%80%93Sith_Empire) "Cold War (Galactic Republic–Sith Empire)"). The Republic and the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order/Legends "Jedi Order/Legends") rebuild and recover over the next [decade](/wiki/Standard_decade/Legends "Standard decade/Legends"), while the Empire secures the territory gained during the war and rebuilds their war machine in preparation for the inevitable resumption of hostilities.[[23]](#cite_note-Encyclopedia-23) By [3643 BBY](/wiki/3643_BBY "3643 BBY"),[[18]](#cite_note-Time_Question-18) the tensions between the Empire and the Republic have begun to boil over, and proxy and side conflicts occurring across the galaxy only serve to inflame these hostilities.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

The [planet](/wiki/Planet/Legends "Planet/Legends") [Ord Mantell](/wiki/Ord_Mantell/Legends "Ord Mantell/Legends") is embroiled in the [Separatist War](/wiki/Separatist_War "Separatist War"), a civil war between the Republic-backed but corrupt government and the [Mantellian Separatist Movement](/wiki/Mantellian_Separatist_Movement "Mantellian Separatist Movement"), which unbeknownst to the Republic is receiving aid from the Sith Empire. Some of the fiercest fighting centers on the island of [Avilatan](/wiki/Avilatan "Avilatan"), which is home to the Republic [garrison](/wiki/Garrison/Legends "Garrison/Legends") [Fort Garnik](/wiki/Fort_Garnik "Fort Garnik") and a number of separatist bases, but many Mantellians are forced to become [refugees](/wiki/Refugee/Legends "Refugee/Legends") as the war drags on.

While making a delivery to Ord Mantell, a [smuggler](/wiki/Voidhound "Voidhound") is double-crossed by the criminal [Skavak](/wiki/Skavak/Legends "Skavak/Legends"), who steals the [smuggler's](/wiki/Smuggler/Legends "Smuggler/Legends") [ship](/wiki/Starship/Legends "Starship/Legends"). The smuggler works with local [crime lord](/wiki/Crime_lord/Legends "Crime lord/Legends") [Viidu](/wiki/Viidu "Viidu") and his [lieutenants](/wiki/Lieutenant/Legends "Lieutenant/Legends"), including the native farmboy [Corso Riggs](/wiki/Corso_Riggs "Corso Riggs"), to track down Skavak, and in the process the smuggler deals significant damage to the separatists' operations. The search culminates in a raid on the [separatist stronghold](/wiki/Separatist_stronghold "Separatist stronghold"), but Skavak is already on his way to Coruscant with the smuggler's ship, thanks to Viidu's traitorous lieutenant [Syreena](/wiki/Syreena "Syreena").

Around the same [time](/wiki/Time/Legends "Time/Legends"), the elite [Special Forces](/wiki/Republic_Special_Forces_Division "Republic Special Forces Division") unit [Havoc Squad](/wiki/Havoc_Squad "Havoc Squad") is on Ord Mantell, and its [newest member](/wiki/Meteor_(Havoc_Squad) "Meteor (Havoc Squad)") joins the [squad's](/wiki/Squad/Legends "Squad/Legends") search for a missing [ZR-57 orbital strike bomb](/wiki/ZR-57_orbital_strike_bomb "ZR-57 orbital strike bomb") that has been stolen by the separatists. Working with the other members of the squad, the [Republic trooper](/wiki/Republic_trooper "Republic trooper") closes in on the [bomb](/wiki/Bomb/Legends "Bomb/Legends"), eliminating several of the separatists leaders in the process, but the rest of the squad goes missing in the separatists' [volcano](/wiki/Mount_Avilatan "Mount Avilatan") stronghold—and when the trooper rushes to the rescue of [Commander](/wiki/Commander/Legends "Commander/Legends") [Harron Tavus](/wiki/Harron_Tavus "Harron Tavus") and the rest of the squad, the [soldier](/wiki/Soldier/Legends "Soldier/Legends") finds that Tavus and the others are traitors who defect to the Empire.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24) With the Republic's recent successes against the separatists,[[25]](#cite_note-Lost_Suns_1-25) the separatists are forced on the defensive and ultimately defeated. The surviving members of the movement flee offworld, finding sanctuary with [Chornarov](/wiki/Chornarov "Chornarov"), the corrupt and power-hungry [governor](/wiki/Governor/Legends "Governor/Legends") of the Republic planet [Cademimu V](/wiki/Cademimu_V "Cademimu V").[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

 [![The new Jedi Temple on Tython](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/Jedi_Temple_Tython.png/revision/latest?cb=20150803132142) [![The new Jedi Temple on Tython](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/Jedi_Temple_Tython.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20150803132142)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/Jedi_Temple_Tython.png/revision/latest?cb=20150803132142) 

The new Jedi Temple on Tython

 

After the destruction of the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple/Legends "Jedi Temple/Legends") on Coruscant during the Sacking, the Jedi Order retreated to its recently rediscovered [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld/Legends "Homeworld/Legends") of [Tython](/wiki/Tython/Legends "Tython/Legends") in the [Deep Core](/wiki/Deep_Core/Legends "Deep Core/Legends"). There, they train a new generation of [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi/Legends "Jedi/Legends") and rediscover their past amongst Tython's verdant [forests](/wiki/Tree/Legends "Tree/Legends") and [mountains](/wiki/Mountain/Legends "Mountain/Legends"), though the violent [Flesh Raiders](/wiki/Flesh_Raider "Flesh Raider") pose a threat to both the Jedi and the illegal [Twi'lek](/wiki/Twi%27lek/Legends "Twi'lek/Legends") settlers of [Kalikori village](/wiki/Kalikori_village "Kalikori village").

The [new Padawan](/wiki/The_Barsen%27thor "The Barsen'thor") of [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master/Legends "Jedi Master/Legends") [Yuon Par](/wiki/Yuon_Par "Yuon Par") discovers that an ancient teaching [hologram](/wiki/Hologram/Legends "Hologram/Legends") has been stolen from Tython's ruins and traces the theft to a villager named [Nalen Raloch](/wiki/Nalen_Raloch "Nalen Raloch"), but Raloch uses his newfound [Force-sensitivity](/wiki/Force-sensitive/Legends "Force-sensitive/Legends") to try and [kill](/wiki/Death/Legends "Death/Legends") the apprentice. Studying the recovered hologram, Par and her student discover the existence of the [Fount of Rajivari](/wiki/Fount_of_Rajivari "Fount of Rajivari"), a collection of knowledge left behind by the ancient Jedi Master [Rajivari](/wiki/Rajivari "Rajivari"). Joining forces with the [Trandoshan](/wiki/Trandoshan/Legends "Trandoshan/Legends") hunter [Qyzen Fess](/wiki/Qyzen_Fess "Qyzen Fess"), the apprentice locates the Fount—discovering it to be Rajivari's own [Force ghost](/wiki/Force_ghost/Legends "Force ghost/Legends")—and prevents a now-insane Raloch from destroying the ancient [Forge](/wiki/Vur_Tepe "Vur Tepe") that the Order used to construct [lightsabers](/wiki/Lightsaber/Legends "Lightsaber/Legends"), thereby earning the rank of [Jedi Consular](/wiki/Jedi_Consular "Jedi Consular")—but Master Par succumbs to a [mysterious illness](/wiki/Dark_Plague "Dark Plague") just after her student is promoted.

A [newly arrived initiate](/wiki/Hero_of_Tython "Hero of Tython") proves vital in halting an [invasion](/wiki/Attack_on_the_Gnarls_Outpost "Attack on the Gnarls Outpost") of the [Tythonian Gnarls](/wiki/Tythonian_Gnarls "Tythonian Gnarls") region by the Flesh Raiders, defeating the [Dark Jedi](/wiki/Dark_Jedi/Legends "Dark Jedi/Legends") [Callef](/wiki/Callef "Callef"), who was leading them in a [duel](/wiki/Duel_in_the_Gnarls_cave "Duel in the Gnarls cave"). The Jedi is taken on as a [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan/Legends "Padawan/Legends") by Master [Orgus Din](/wiki/Orgus_Din "Orgus Din"), and the two investigate the Flesh Raiders' recent activities. When Din and his student discover that Din's former apprentice [Bengel Morr](/wiki/Bengel_Morr "Bengel Morr") is leading the Flesh Raiders, the Jedi launch attacks on the Flesh Raiders across Tython, but Din is captured by Morr after he is betrayed by Kalikori village. His apprentice—after escaping another trap set by the villagers—pursues Morr with the [astromech droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid/Legends "Astromech droid/Legends") [T7-O1](/wiki/T7-O1 "T7-O1") and ultimately defeats him in [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Forge "Battle of the Forge") at the Forge, rescuing Din and earning the rank of [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight/Legends "Jedi Knight/Legends").[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

 [![The tomb of Tulak Hord, one of many tombs on Korriban](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Tomb_of_Tulak_Hord.png/revision/latest?cb=20150731132430) [![The tomb of Tulak Hord, one of many tombs on Korriban](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Tomb_of_Tulak_Hord.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20150731132430)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/Tomb_of_Tulak_Hord.png/revision/latest?cb=20150731132430) 

The tomb of Tulak Hord, one of many tombs on Korriban

 

On the [Sith](/wiki/Sith/Legends "Sith/Legends") world of [Korriban](/wiki/Korriban/Legends "Korriban/Legends"), [Sith acolytes](/wiki/Sith_acolyte/Legends "Sith acolyte/Legends") study at the [Sith Academy](/wiki/Sith_Academy_(Korriban) "Sith Academy (Korriban)") and compete to become the apprentices of powerful [Sith Lords](/wiki/Sith_Lord/Legends "Sith Lord/Legends"). Excavation of the tombs in the [Valley of the Dark Lords](/wiki/Valley_of_the_Dark_Lords/Legends "Valley of the Dark Lords/Legends") continues, despite the prevalence of creatures such as [shyracks](/wiki/Shyrack/Legends "Shyrack/Legends"), [k'lor'slugs](/wiki/K%27lor%27slug/Legends "K'lor'slug/Legends"), and [tuk'ata](/wiki/Tuk%27ata/Legends "Tuk'ata/Legends"), and a group of rebellious [slaves](/wiki/Slavery/Legends "Slavery/Legends") has taken refuge in one of the tombs. Some of the Academy's instructors, disgusted by the Empire's recent decision to allow slaves and [aliens](/wiki/Alien/Legends "Alien/Legends") to be trained as Sith, do their best to ensure purity in the blood of their students. A [recently arrived slave](/wiki/Darth_Nox "Darth Nox") joins a group of acolytes under [Overseer](/wiki/Overseer_(Sith) "Overseer (Sith)") [Harkun](/wiki/Harkun "Harkun"), who is determined to see the slave fail, and the acolytes undergo a series of tests in the Academy and amid the tombs of the Valley. Harkun's students are competing to become the apprentice of the Sith Lord [Zash](/wiki/Darth_Zash "Darth Zash"), and the overseer is enraged to witness the slave complete each test perfectly—so he arranges for two acolytes to kill the slave and thereby assure that the [pureblooded](/wiki/Sith_(species)/Legends "Sith (species)/Legends") acolyte [Ffon Althe](/wiki/Ffon_Althe "Ffon Althe") becomes Zash's apprentice. Harkun's attempt fails, and the slave also manages to awaken the [Dashade](/wiki/Dashade/Legends "Dashade/Legends") [Shadow Killer](/wiki/Shadow_Killer "Shadow Killer") [Khem Val](/wiki/Khem_Val "Khem Val"), who is forced to swear loyalty to the acolyte after being defeated. Impressed by the acolyte's accomplishments, Zash takes the former slave as her apprentice, though the apprentice is quickly caught up in the rivalry between Zash and her superior, [Darth Skotia](/wiki/Darth_Skotia "Darth Skotia").

Around the same time, a [new acolyte](/wiki/Empire%27s_Wrath "Empire's Wrath") is placed under the tutelage of Overseer [Tremel](/wiki/Tremel "Tremel"), who seeks to use his new student to destroy the acolyte [Vemrin](/wiki/Vemrin "Vemrin")—a potential apprentice to the Sith Lord [Darth Baras](/wiki/Darth_Baras "Darth Baras"). Tremel's student completes each of the tests set by the overseer, but Baras confronts the acolyte and reveals that Tremel is rushing the student's instruction to achieve his own goals. At Baras's instruction, the acolyte turns on Tremel and slays him, earning Baras's favor and becoming a possibility for a new apprentice. The acolyte's final test is to retrieve an ancient lightsaber from the [tomb](/wiki/Tomb_of_Naga_Sadow "Tomb of Naga Sadow") of the Sith Lord [Naga Sadow](/wiki/Naga_Sadow/Legends "Naga Sadow/Legends"), and after using the Twi'lek treasure hunter and slave [Vette](/wiki/Vette "Vette") to navigate the tomb, the student defeats Vemrin and secures a place as Baras's apprentice.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

The industrial planet [Nal Hutta](/wiki/Nal_Hutta/Legends "Nal Hutta/Legends"), adopted homeworld of the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt/Legends "Hutt/Legends") [species](/wiki/Species/Legends "Species/Legends"), is rife with crime and conflict between rival members of the [Hutt Cartel](/wiki/Hutt_Cartel/Legends "Hutt Cartel/Legends"), including [Voontara Fa'athra](/wiki/Voontara_Fa%27athra "Voontara Fa'athra") and [Suudaa Nem'ro](/wiki/Suudaa_Nem%27ro "Suudaa Nem'ro"). The native [Evocii](/wiki/Evocii "Evocii") species, who have long been disenfranchised by their Hutt rulers, struggle alongside [Human](/wiki/Human/Legends "Human/Legends") and alien workers as they toil in the toxic [swamps](/wiki/Swamp/Legends "Swamp/Legends") and industrial facilities that crowd the planet's surface, though some [mercenaries](/wiki/Mercenary/Legends "Mercenary/Legends"), criminals, and radical Evocii wage guerrilla wars against the Hutts and anyone else they encounter. As the [Great Hunt](/wiki/Great_Hunt_(competition) "Great Hunt (competition)"), a major [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian/Legends "Mandalorian/Legends") [bounty hunting](/wiki/Bounty_hunter/Legends "Bounty hunter/Legends") competition, draws near, the veteran hunter [Braden](/wiki/Braden "Braden") mentors a [young hunter](/wiki/Hunter_(individual) "Hunter (individual)") and seeks to secure sponsorship from Nem'ro the Hutt in order for his protege to enter the competition. With the help of Braden, a young [slicer](/wiki/Slicer/Legends "Slicer/Legends") named [Mako](/wiki/Mako_(slicer) "Mako (slicer)"), and Braden's associate [Jory](/wiki/Jory "Jory"), the hunter tracks down and kills the criminal [Vexx](/wiki/Vexx "Vexx")—but returns to find Braden and Jory murdered by a rival hunter named [Tarro Blood](/wiki/Tarro_Blood "Tarro Blood"). Despite their deaths, the hunter and Mako continue their efforts to secure sponsorship, completing a number of [bounties](/wiki/Bounty/Legends "Bounty/Legends") for Nem'ro. However, Nem'ro double-crosses the hunter, giving his sponsorship to a Trandoshan named [Rarsk](/wiki/Rarsk "Rarsk") and challenging the hunter to go and take the sponsorship from Rarsk. Nem'ro is greatly pleased by the hunter's success in doing so, and agrees to officially sponsor the hunter in the Great Hunt, which will begin on the Imperial capital of [Dromund Kaas](/wiki/Dromund_Kaas/Legends "Dromund Kaas/Legends").

Also in Nem'ro's industrial town of [Jiguuna](/wiki/Jiguuna "Jiguuna"), an [operative](/wiki/Cipher_Nine "Cipher Nine") of the Sith Empire's [Imperial Intelligence](/wiki/Imperial_Intelligence_(Sith_Empire) "Imperial Intelligence (Sith Empire)") is tasked with securing an alliance between the Empire and Nem'ro, who is a powerful member of the Hutt Cartel. Adopting the identity of the notorious [pirate](/wiki/Pirate/Legends "Pirate/Legends") known as the [Red Blade](/wiki/Red_Blade "Red Blade"), the agent attempts to earn the trust of [Karrels Javis](/wiki/Karrels_Javis "Karrels Javis"), one of Nem'ro's lieutenants, and completes a number of sabotage missions against the operations of Nem'ro's rival Fa'athra. However, the agent is forced to find a new ally when Javis's sons are involved in an incident with a Sith that leaves [one son](/wiki/Serjil_Javis "Serjil Javis") dead and the [other](/wiki/Vargai_Javis "Vargai Javis") crippled, and Javis is eliminated as a loose end. The [Rattataki](/wiki/Rattataki/Legends "Rattataki/Legends") mercenary [Kaliyo Djannis](/wiki/Kaliyo_Djannis "Kaliyo Djannis") becomes suspicious of "the Red Blade," but allies herself with the agent nonetheless upon discovering the operative's true allegiance, and aids the agent in manufacturing evidence that Fa'athra is colluding with the Republic. Nem'ro is successfully persuaded into allying with the Empire, and though the real Red Blade arrives on Hutta shortly before the agent departs, the operative kills the pirate to secure the operation, and is recalled to Dromund Kaas with Djannis.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

[Grand Moff](/wiki/Grand_Moff/Legends "Grand Moff/Legends") [Rycus Kilran](/wiki/Rycus_Kilran "Rycus Kilran") is eager to restart the war, and his efforts to [recapture](/wiki/Attack_on_the_Brentaal_Star "Attack on the Brentaal Star") a defecting [Imperial general](/wiki/The_General "The General") is a success despite the loss of a number of ships to Republic forces under [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master/Legends "Grand Master/Legends") [Satele Shan](/wiki/Satele_Shan "Satele Shan"). Kilran's efforts to capture the Republic [ambassador](/wiki/Ambassador/Legends "Ambassador/Legends") [Vyn Asara](/wiki/Vyn_Asara "Vyn Asara") by [attacking](/wiki/Assault_on_the_Esseles "Assault on the Esseles") the transport [*Esseles*](/wiki/Esseles_(starship) "Esseles (starship)") fails,[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24) however, forcing Imperial spokespeople to deny the Empire's involvement in an effort to distance themselves from the incident.[[25]](#cite_note-Lost_Suns_1-25) Amid the many proxy conflicts, the Empire and Republic begin to engage each other in encounters that come closer and closer to open war. The xenophobic [Advozse Hegemony](/wiki/Advozse_Hegemony "Advozse Hegemony") acquires the powerful [battle station](/wiki/Battle_station/Legends "Battle station/Legends") known as [Hammer Station](/wiki/Hammer_Station "Hammer Station") and attempts to expand their territory, but the galactic powers dispatch forces to destroy the station. A similar conflict arises when the Mandalorian [Clan Varad](/wiki/Clan_Varad "Clan Varad") begins terrorizing the Outer Rim with the stolen Republic warship *[Allusis](/wiki/Allusis "Allusis")*; both governments send strike teams to destroy Clan Varad and take control of the *Allusis*.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

 [![Coruscant security fights criminals for control of the recovering capital.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7b/Marketskirmish.png/revision/latest?cb=20120421172950) [![Coruscant security fights criminals for control of the recovering capital.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7b/Marketskirmish.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20120421172950)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7b/Marketskirmish.png/revision/latest?cb=20120421172950) 

Coruscant security fights criminals for control of the recovering capital.

 

The Republic capital of Coruscant is still recovering from the Sacking a decade prior, and though [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor/Legends "Supreme Chancellor/Legends") [Dorian Janarus](/wiki/Dorian_Janarus "Dorian Janarus") and [Senator](/wiki/Senator/Legends "Senator/Legends") [Vanara Kayl](/wiki/Vanara_Kayl "Vanara Kayl") have led efforts to rebuild [Galactic City](/wiki/Galactic_City/Legends "Galactic City/Legends"), gangs such as the [Migrant Merchants' Guild](/wiki/Migrant_Merchants%27_Guild "Migrant Merchants' Guild") and [Black Sun](/wiki/Black_Sun/Legends "Black Sun/Legends") control entire sectors of the capital, and the [Coruscant Security Force](/wiki/Coruscant_Security_Force/Legends "Coruscant Security Force/Legends") receives no help from the Imperial-backed vigilante group known as the [Justicars' Brigade](/wiki/Justicars%27_Brigade "Justicars' Brigade"). Unbeknownst to the Republic, the Empire has more than just monetary influence on the capital: Imperial forces are searching the ruins of the Jedi Temple for artifacts and knowledge left behind in the building's destruction.

Yuon Par's apprentice, now a full-fledged Jedi Consular, comes to Coruscant in search of the [Noetikons](/wiki/Noetikon "Noetikon"), ancient Jedi artifacts that could prove vital in healing Par of the mysterious illness that struck her on Tython. Fighting through various elements of Coruscant's underworld to retrieve the three devices across Coruscant, the Consular consults the Noetikons and learns of a [shielding technique](/wiki/Shielding_technique "Shielding technique") that successfully heals Par of her illness. However, the threat does not end there: it soon becomes apparent that the "Dark Plague" that had afflicted Par has also infected several Jedi Masters across the galaxy.

Havoc Squad's newest member, who is now the only remaining loyal member of the unit, is recalled to Coruscant with Lieutenant [Aric Jorgan](/wiki/Aric_Jorgan "Aric Jorgan") by [General](/wiki/General/Legends "General/Legends") [Elin Garza](/wiki/Elin_Garza "Elin Garza") of SpecForce Division. There, the loyal trooper is given command of the unit as a lieutenant, Havoc Squad is reformed with the trooper and Jorgan as its first members, and Garza tasks the squad with hunting down the traitors amid an inquiry by the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate/Legends "Galactic Senate/Legends") into the recent [mass defections](/wiki/SpecForce_Incident "SpecForce Incident") in SpecForce. Following leads on the traitors' allies across Coruscant, Havoc Squad finally locates and defeats [Jek Kardan](/wiki/Jek_Kardan "Jek Kardan"), one of the founders of Havoc Squad and Tavus's mentor, but is then sent to rescue Senator [Zorin Krasul](/wiki/Zorin_Krasul "Zorin Krasul") when he is kidnapped by the Havoc traitor [Wraith](/wiki/Zora "Zora"). Havoc Squad manages to rescue Krasul from the [space station](/wiki/Space_station/Legends "Space station/Legends") [Port Raga](/wiki/Port_Raga "Port Raga"), though the unit fails to capture Wraith.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

The smuggler whose ship Skavak stole on Ord Mantell pursues the "Jackal of the Stars" to Coruscant with Corso Riggs, who sets up a meeting with the [gambler](/wiki/Gambler/Legends "Gambler/Legends") and [information broker](/wiki/Information_broker/Legends "Information broker/Legends") [Darmas Pollaran](/wiki/Darmas_Pollaran "Darmas Pollaran") in hopes of locating Skavak. With Pollaran's help, the smuggler and Riggs chase down leads on Skavak's location in various districts of the galactic capital, tangling with the Migrant Merchants' Guild and Black Sun in the process. After pursuing a lead in Justicar territory, the duo learn of a meeting between Skavak and Imperials in [the Works](/wiki/The_Works/Legends "The Works/Legends") region; the pair crash the meeting, but Skavak escapes in the confusion. However, Skavak lets slip the location of the smuggler's ship, and the captain beats Skavak back to the freighter—only to find a mysterious woman named [Risha](/wiki/Risha_Drayen "Risha Drayen") waiting in the hold.

Orgus Din and his student, now a Jedi Knight, are called to Coruscant to aid in the search for a mysterious darkness that the Jedi have sensed on the capital. However, the young Knight soon becomes involved in the efforts to retrieve the stolen [Planet Prison](/wiki/Planet_Prison "Planet Prison") [superweapon](/wiki/Superweapon/Legends "Superweapon/Legends") as well as its creator, [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor/Legends "Doctor/Legends") [Eli Tarnis](/wiki/Tarnis_(Sith_Lord) "Tarnis (Sith Lord)"), from various gangs across the [city](/wiki/City/Legends "City/Legends"). To the Republic's surprise, it soon becomes apparent that Tarnis is actually a Sith Lord who has infiltrated the Republic's [superweapon development program](/wiki/Republic_superweapon_initiative "Republic superweapon initiative"), and the Knight joins forces with Padawan [Kira Carsen](/wiki/Kira_Carsen "Kira Carsen") in a race against time to prevent Tarnis from using the Planet Prison against Coruscant—but the Knight's success comes with a cost: Tarnis's [father](/wiki/Parent/Legends "Parent/Legends") [Darth Angral](/wiki/Darth_Angral "Darth Angral") declares a personal war on the Republic in response to his son's death at the Jedi's hand. Taking on Carsen as a Padawan, the Knight is sent to Ord Mantell to investigate an [Imperial listening post](/wiki/Imperial_Listening_Post "Imperial Listening Post"), where T7-O1 and the Jedi recover information on something called the "[Desolator](/wiki/Desolator_(superweapon) "Desolator (superweapon)")" that Angral is building.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

 [![The Imperial Citadel in Kaas City, the heart of the Empire](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a9/Imperial_Citadel.png/revision/latest?cb=20150727030751) [![The Imperial Citadel in Kaas City, the heart of the Empire](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a9/Imperial_Citadel.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20150727030751)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a9/Imperial_Citadel.png/revision/latest?cb=20150727030751) 

The Imperial Citadel in Kaas City, the heart of the Empire

 

In contrast to Coruscant, the Imperial capital of Dromund Kaas remains largely under the firm rule of the Empire, though a number of growing threats have begun to undermine Imperial authority. The secretive [Order of Revan](/wiki/Order_of_Revan "Order of Revan") seeks to spread their philosophies throughout the Empire despite the Dark Council's dedication to eradicating the group, and the Sith Lord [Qet](/wiki/Qet "Qet")'s effort to construct a [monument](/wiki/Unfinished_colossus "Unfinished colossus") to his master [Darth Vowrawn](/wiki/Darth_Vowrawn "Darth Vowrawn") went awry when the slave workers [launched a rebellion](/wiki/Dromund_Kaas_rebellion "Dromund Kaas rebellion"). The Sith Lord [Grathan](/wiki/Grathan "Grathan") has recently declared himself the thirteenth Dark Council member, and has fortified his [estate](/wiki/Lord_Grathan%27s_estate "Lord Grathan's estate") with a veritable army. The wild animals that inhabit Dromund Kaas's dark jungles still pose threats outside of the walls of Imperial cities such as the capital of [Kaas City](/wiki/Kaas_City "Kaas City"), and the [Dark Temple](/wiki/Dark_Temple "Dark Temple")—a Sith structure that was used to contain powerful artifacts and the bodies of the Emperor's enemies before it was sealed hundreds of years earlier—has been breached by a group of arrogant Sith Lords who quickly met their death inside; the power of the [dark side](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force/Legends "Dark side of the Force/Legends") has unleashed madness and unspeakable horrors from within the forbidden structure, and the Empire is struggling to contain the Temple's influence.

On Dromund Kaas, Braden's protege arrives along with a half dozen other hunters to learn that there is one spot left in the Great Hunt. Assigned a handler named [Crysta Markon](/wiki/Crysta_Markon "Crysta Markon"), the hunter is tasked with hunting down three targets on the Imperial capital in order to qualify for the [Grand Melee](/wiki/Grand_Melee "Grand Melee") that will decide who enters the Hunt. Tarro Blood, who has already secured a place in the Hunt, repeatedly attempts to sabotage his rival, but despite the interference the hunter successfully completes the three contracts: a Republic noble named [Altaca](/wiki/Altaca "Altaca"), Grathan's apprentice [Vereta Fraabaal](/wiki/Vereta_Fraabaal "Vereta Fraabaal"), and the commander of an Imperial team sent into the Dark Temple. The hunter emerges victorious in the Grand Melee, securing the last spot in the Grand Hunt, and successfully steals a [D5-*Mantis* Patrol Craft](/wiki/D5-Mantis_Patrol_Craft "D5-Mantis Patrol Craft") to use as the hunter's own ship as part of a Great Hunt tradition.

Upon arriving at Imperial Intelligence, the Intelligence operative is debriefed by [Keeper](/wiki/Minister_of_Intelligence_(Galactic_War) "Minister of Intelligence (Galactic War)"), the head of Intelligence's [Operations Division](/wiki/Operations_Division "Operations Division"), and meets [Darth Jadus](/wiki/Darth_Jadus "Darth Jadus"), the Dark Councilor who commands Imperial Intelligence. Assigned a handler in [Watcher Two](/wiki/Shara_Jenn "Shara Jenn"), the agent and Djannis are tasked with rooting out a terrorist cell that is supposedly planning an attack on Dromund Kaas, and interrogation of rebel slaves points to a scientist named [Theovor Mindak](/wiki/Theovor_Mindak "Theovor Mindak") who is in the service of Lord Grathan. With the help of Mindak's daughter [Samara](/wiki/Samara_Mindak "Samara Mindak"), the operative infiltrates Grathan's estate and learns from Mindak that the terrorists plan to detonate the power conduits beneath the Dark Temple—a detonation that would severely damage Kaas City. The operative successfully stops the terrorists, but the terrorists strike a blow against the Empire nonetheless: Darth Jadus and thousands of people are killed when Jadus's flagship is destroyed by terrorists led by the mysterious "[Eagle](/wiki/Eagle "Eagle")." The operative is then promoted to the rank of [Cipher Agent](/wiki/Cipher_Agent "Cipher Agent"), and "Cipher Nine" is tasked with rooting out and destroying the Eagle's terrorist network.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

### Chapter 1

:   "*Seven battle cruisers are en route to disputed sectors. They will reclaim our territories within the hour. Imperial Intelligence has arrested over nine hundred dissidents on Sullust and Bothawui. The dissidents will be tried, judged and executed. This is a warning to those who oppose us—and an invitation to those who would join us. The Empire abides by the Treaty of Coruscant. But should the Republic begin the war again, we will strike without mercy… and the time for choosing sides will be over.*"
:   ―An Imperial propaganda speech broadcast near the end of the Cold War[[9]](#cite_note-Manual-9)

The planet [Taris](/wiki/Taris/Legends "Taris/Legends") was destroyed three hundred years earlier by the Sith Lord [Darth Malak](/wiki/Darth_Malak "Darth Malak"), and the once great city-world was turned to ruins that have been overgrown by Taris's recovering ecosystem in the last few centuries. In the absence of settlers, Taris's environment has recovered from years of industrial pollution, though some of the planet's wildlife has been affected by the pollution and radiation. The Republic has recently begun a [resettlement initiative](/wiki/Taris_Resettlement_Initiative "Taris Resettlement Initiative") under the [Taris Reconstruction Authority](/wiki/Taris_Reconstruction_Authority "Taris Reconstruction Authority") and Governor [Leontyne Saresh](/wiki/Leontyne_Saresh "Leontyne Saresh"), though pirates, scavengers, corruption, [rakghouls](/wiki/Rakghoul "Rakghoul"), and a number of other setbacks have impeded progress. The [Republic Military](/wiki/Republic_Military/Legends "Republic Military/Legends") maintains outposts in the wilderness, though it is unsafe for colonists to travel outside of the [Republic Resettlement Zone](/wiki/Republic_Resettlement_Zone "Republic Resettlement Zone"), and the initiative's headquarters at [Olaris](/wiki/Olaris "Olaris") is frequently besieged by rakghouls.

In the far reaches of the world, Republic scientists also make a disturbing discovery—a new species of rakghoul called the [nekghoul](/wiki/Nekghoul "Nekghoul") has evolved, one that is Force-sensitive and intelligent. The Jedi Knight and company are sent to Taris to locate [Doctor](/wiki/Doctor/Legends "Doctor/Legends") [Nasan Godera](/wiki/Nasan_Godera "Nasan Godera"), a brilliant Republic [scientist](/wiki/Scientist/Legends "Scientist/Legends") who quit the Republic in disgust after the Sacking of Coruscant; however, Imperial Intelligence is already one step ahead of the Knight, forcing the Jedi to pursue Intelligence's [Watcher One](/wiki/Watcher_One "Watcher One") across Taris in a race to locate and then rescue Godera from the Empire. The Knight succeeds, but not before Watcher One is able to extract valuable information from the scientist on the subject of superweapons.

The first of the infected Masters is the [Kaleesh](/wiki/Kaleesh/Legends "Kaleesh/Legends") [Cin Tykan](/wiki/Cin_Tykan "Cin Tykan"), who had been assisting the Republic in the exploration and resettlement of Taris with his Padawan [Aris Vauranelle](/wiki/Aris_Vauranelle "Aris Vauranelle") before he was overcome by the plague's madness. Tracking down Tykan, the Consular rescued Tykan's expedition from the death-trap he had led them into, and discovered that Tykan intended to destroy Taris's ruined [reactors](/wiki/Reactor/Legends "Reactor/Legends") and infrastructure in order to wipe out the resettlement project. The Consular foiled Tykan's efforts, however, ending the Jedi Master's madness.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

The planet [Balmorra](/wiki/Balmorra/Legends "Balmorra/Legends") is suffering under an Imperial occupation that has lasted for almost three decades, and much of the world's infrastructure and surface is heavily damaged from the years of warfare. The Imperials are fighting an ineffective battle against the [Balmorran resistance](/wiki/Balmorran_resistance "Balmorran resistance"), though the rebels lack the strength to drive the Empire off their homeworld themselves. However, the Republic Military and the Jedi Order have begun secretly lending their support to the resistance, and despite the Balmorrans' resentment of the Republic's abandonment of their planet at the end of the Great War, they have begun to make progress—but the arrival of [Darth Lachris](/wiki/Darth_Lachris "Darth Lachris"), the new Sith governor, begins an increased crackdown on the resistance. Lachris's forces uncover and foil a Republic invasion attempt, forcing the Republic to declare that the Jedi and Republic Military forces who participated to be rogue agents.

Balmorra is also the site of one of the Great Hunt targets—each competitor in the Great Hunt is assigned a target that they must eliminate or capture, but they must also compete against another hunter who is given the same target. Mako and the hunter's first target is [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral/Legends "Admiral/Legends") [Ivernus](/wiki/Ivernus "Ivernus"), who is stationed at Balmorra but never leaves his [flagship](/wiki/Flagship/Legends "Flagship/Legends"), so the pair offer their services to [Lieutenant Major](/wiki/Lieutenant_Major "Lieutenant Major") [Pirrell](/wiki/Pirrell "Pirrell"), a subordinate of the admiral, in hopes of getting close to their target. Pirrell uses the bounty hunter to sabotage various Imperial operations on the war-torn world in order to discredit his incompetent superior [Colonel](/wiki/Colonel/Legends "Colonel/Legends") [Sartius](/wiki/Sartius "Sartius"), and his plan successfully brings the admiral to the capital of [Sobrik](/wiki/Sobrik "Sobrik"). Pirrell's [Cathar](/wiki/Cathar/Legends "Cathar/Legends") companion [Murghir](/wiki/Murghir "Murghir") reveals herself as the hunter's competition and tries to take down Ivernus, but the hunter kills both Ivernus and Murghir in the firefight and advances in the Great Hunt.

As the first step in tracking down the culprits responsible for the *Dominator*'s destruction, Cipher Nine is sent to Balmorra and tasked with infiltrating a cell of terrorists led by the mysterious [Gray Star](/wiki/Gray_Star "Gray Star"). With the help of Sanju Pyne, Cipher Nine performs several missions for the resistance in order to win the trust of Gray Star's lieutenant [Chemish Or](/wiki/Chemish_Or "Chemish Or"); however, Or becomes suspicious of Pyne and kills him. Cipher Nine's cover remains intact, and Or sends the operative to extract Gray Star from the Balmorran Arms Factory—where the operative learns that Gray Star is a soldier in the Republic Army, and successfully eliminates the resistance leader.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

The moon of [Nar Shaddaa](/wiki/Nar_Shaddaa/Legends "Nar Shaddaa/Legends") is a hotbed of covert activity, as the Hutts' neutrality forces both the Empire and the Republic to coexist in a relatively peaceful fashion there. In the shadows, however, the [Republic Strategic Information Service](/wiki/Republic_Strategic_Information_Service "Republic Strategic Information Service") (SIS) and Imperial Intelligence are locked in a battle for supremacy, and the Empire maintains secret facilities such as the [prison](/wiki/Prison/Legends "Prison/Legends") district of [Shadow Town](/wiki/Shadow_Town "Shadow Town"). Gangs such as the [Kintan Kings](/wiki/Kintan_Kings "Kintan Kings") battle the [Exchange](/wiki/Exchange "Exchange"), the Hutt Cartel, and other criminal organizations for control of Nar Shaddaa, and the Empire's rule over parts of the moon is challenged by many of the immigrants and war refugees who inhabit areas such as the [Corellian](/wiki/Corellian_Sector_(Nar_Shaddaa)/Legends "Corellian Sector (Nar Shaddaa)/Legends") and [Duros Sectors](/wiki/Duros_Sector "Duros Sector").

General Suthra dispatches the Jedi Knight to Nar Shaddaa to secure the [Power Guard Project](/wiki/Power_Guard_Enhancement_System "Power Guard Enhancement System"), an experimental supersoldier program run in secret by the Republic on the moon, and the Knight works with the local Strategic Information Service agents to track down the SIS agent [Galen](/wiki/Galen_(SIS) "Galen (SIS)"), who went missing while searching for the program. However, the Knight soon discovers that Angral's apprentice [Sadic](/wiki/Sadic "Sadic") has taken control of the program, leading the Knight to pursue Sadic and the Power Guard program across the moon. Sadic destroys the [SIS base](/wiki/SIS_safe_house "SIS safe house") with Power Guards, but the Knight nonetheless tracks him back to the prison district of Shadow Town, where Sadic—who has undergone the Power Guard process himself out of a desire for power—is killed by the Jedi.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

Nar Shaddaa is also the location of the Jedi Master [Duras Fain](/wiki/Duras_Fain "Duras Fain"), who is suspected of being infected with the Dark Plague and responsible for the fanatical criminal cult known as the [Guiding Hand](/wiki/Guiding_Hand "Guiding Hand") that has recently come to power on Nar Shaddaa. The Jedi Consular seeks out Master Bakarn's contact, the eccentric scientist [Tharan Cedrax](/wiki/Tharan_Cedrax "Tharan Cedrax") and his holographic assistant [Holiday](/wiki/Holiday_(hologram) "Holiday (hologram)"), and rescued Cedrax from a Guiding Hand attack in the [Nikto Sector](/wiki/Nikto_Sector "Nikto Sector"). With Cedrax's help, the Consular infiltrates the tech specialists known as the [Red Light Lancers](/wiki/Red_Light_Lancers "Red Light Lancers"), and ultimately tracks down Fain in Shadow Town. Thanks to Cedrax's [inventions](/wiki/Tharan_Cedrax%27s_anti-mind_control_device "Tharan Cedrax's anti-mind control device"), the Consular resists Fain's mind control attempt and defeats the crazed Jedi Master before freeing him from the effects of the plague—and the cured Fain reveals that the infected Masters were part of an ill-fated [expedition](/wiki/Malachor_III_Expedition "Malachor III Expedition") to the planet [Malachor III](/wiki/Malachor_III "Malachor III") in their youth.

The hunter's next target is on Nar Shadda: the [Eidolon](/wiki/Eidolon_(assassin) "Eidolon (assassin)"), a notorious [assassin](/wiki/Assassin/Legends "Assassin/Legends") who heads the Republic-allied [Eidolon Security](/wiki/Eidolon_Security "Eidolon Security") company. With the help of a Hutt Cartel lieutenant named [Gele'ren](/wiki/Gele%27ren "Gele'ren") and Mako's childhood friend [Anuli](/wiki/Anuli "Anuli"), the hunter attacks the Eidolon's corporate holdings in an attempt to draw the target out. The hunter's competition, a [clan](/wiki/Zargnor_Clan "Zargnor Clan") of [Ugnaughts](/wiki/Ugnaught/Legends "Ugnaught/Legends"), are easily dispatched, but the Eidolon kills Anuli and leaves [assassin droids](/wiki/Assassin_droid/Legends "Assassin droid/Legends") to kill the hunter. To the Eidolon's surprise, Mako and the hunter survive and pursue him to a [safe house](/wiki/Eidolon%27s_safe_house "Eidolon's safe house"), where they successfully take down their target.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

After Sadic's defeat, General Suthra dispatches the Knight and Kira Carsen to meet with a potential defector named Admiral [Hacklin](/wiki/Hacklin "Hacklin"), but the meeting is a trap set by [Valis](/wiki/Valis "Valis"), a "[Child](/wiki/Children_of_the_Emperor "Children of the Emperor")" of the Sith Emperor. Valis seeks to recapture Carsen, herself a former Child who escaped the Empire, though Valis is defeated by the two Jedi.

After Cedrax joins the Jedi Consular's crew on Nar Shaddaa, the Jedi rushes to defuse the situation aboard the Republic vessel [*Carida*](/wiki/Carida_(starship) "Carida (starship)"), where a Jedi Knight named [Laranna Fain](/wiki/Laranna_Fain "Laranna Fain")—Duras Fain's daughter—has seemingly gone insane. After fighting off an Imperial ambush during which Fain had been injured, the *Carida* had been visited by a mysterious Jedi Master who "healed" the injured Jedi and departed—after which Fain started attacking everyone. The Consular ultimately heals Fain of the plague's influence, and learned that the "Jedi Master" responsible for the plague is actually a Jedi-turned-Sith named [Vivicar](/wiki/Parkanas_Tark "Parkanas Tark") who can only infect those he has personal contact with.

After taking down the Eidolon, the hunter and Mako are surprised to be recalled to Dromund Kaas by Huntmaster Assistant [Lek](/wiki/Lek "Lek"), who sends the pair on a discreet assignment to locate and eliminate a [slicer](/wiki/Bilikin_Drell "Bilikin Drell") who stole the Great Hunt target list and is auctioning it on Nal Hutta. Before his death, the slicer reveals he was hired by a Mandalorian, and the hunter suspects Tarro Blood, whose targets were excluded from the stolen list.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

The [desert](/wiki/Desert/Legends "Desert/Legends") world of [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine/Legends "Tatooine/Legends") is another world where the Empire and the Republic work behind the scenes to gain an advantage over each other, with the Republic supporting the civilian inhabitants of [Anchorhead](/wiki/Anchorhead/Legends "Anchorhead/Legends") and other settlements, while the Empire has established a garrison in the town of [Mos Ila](/wiki/Mos_Ila "Mos Ila"). The [Imperial Reclamation Service](/wiki/Imperial_Reclamation_Service "Imperial Reclamation Service") scours the desert for artifacts, and the Republic Military and the Imperial Military are forced to engage pirates, the native [Sand People](/wiki/Tusken_Raider/Legends "Tusken Raider/Legends"), mercenaries, various alien species, and Tatooine's hostile wildlife. The [Czerka Corporation](/wiki/Czerka_Arms/Legends "Czerka Arms/Legends") uncovers a [powerful artifact](/wiki/The_Imprisoned_One "The Imprisoned One") of the [Rakata](/wiki/Rakata/Legends "Rakata/Legends") species in the [Dune Sea](/wiki/Dune_Sea/Legends "Dune Sea/Legends"), sparking a race between the two galactic powers to take control of the artifact or to destroy it before its influence spreads.

A similar situation arises when a Republic survey team accidentally awakens the servants of the mad Sith Lord [Vodal Kressh](/wiki/Vodal_Kressh "Vodal Kressh") on [Athiss](/wiki/Athiss/Legends "Athiss/Legends"), though either the Republic or the Empire is able to destroy Kressh's servants and end the threat his power poses to the galaxy.

Sent to Tatooine, the hunter is tasked with tracking down the notorious [Devaronian](/wiki/Devaronian/Legends "Devaronian/Legends") conman [Tyresius Lokai](/wiki/Gault_Rennow "Gault Rennow"), but an attempt to capture Lokai—who is posing as "Gellar Roing"—in the [Mos Ila Spaceport](/wiki/Mos_Ila_Spaceport "Mos Ila Spaceport") sees Lokai escape. Learning that the other competitor targeting Lokai, [Veeboo Lunx](/wiki/Veeboo_Lunx "Veeboo Lunx"), was bribed by Lokai to drop out of the Hunt after shooting down the conman's ship, the hunter tracks down and eliminates Lunx before pursuing Lokai across the desert. Lokai is unable to repair his damaged ship before the hunter arrives, but after a firefight, Lokai offers his services to the hunter and uses a genetically identical body double as proof of Lokai's death. Changing his name to Gault Rennow, the Devaronian joins the hunter's crew.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

The Jedi Knight's next assignment is to locate the [Shock Drum](/wiki/Shock_Drum "Shock Drum") weapon on Tatooine, but like the Power Guard Project, the Shock Drum has already been seized by Angral's apprentice [Praven](/wiki/Praven "Praven"). The honorable Sith challenges the Jedi to a [duel](/wiki/Duel_on_the_Esus_Mesa "Duel on the Esus Mesa") for the Shock Drum control codes, as he finds Angral's command to activate the seismic superweapon to be dishonorable. After the Jedi emerges victorious, the Knight rushes to save Carsen's former Jedi Master [Bela Kiwiiks](/wiki/Bela_Kiwiiks "Bela Kiwiiks"), who Angral ordered Praven to leave for dead with the Shock Drum; fighting through the fearsome creatures known as [sand demons](/wiki/Sand_demon "Sand demon"), the Knight manages to rescue Kiwiiks and disarm the Shock Drum before it destabilizes the planet's core.

The Consular's next mission is to find and cure Master [Eriz Vossan](/wiki/Eriz_Vossan "Eriz Vossan") on Tatooine, and the Jedi retraces Vossan's steps in hopes of locating the Jedi Master. The Consular encounters a group of [Jawas](/wiki/Jawa/Legends "Jawa/Legends") whom Vossan had visited, only to find that the Jedi had convinced them to try and take control of the desert with war droids. The Consular soon discovers that Vossan, in his madness, believes Tatooine's Sand People to be "the ultimate warriors," and that Vossan has gone in search of a particularly warlike tribe. The Consular finds Vossan deep in the desert with the Sand People, and after healing the Master, learns more about the expedition to Malachor. The Padawans who went to Malachor had been overcome by something evil they discovered, and in their haste to escape, one of the Padawans, Parkanas Tark, was left behind by his fellows.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

The Core World of [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan/Legends "Alderaan/Legends"), a founding world of the Republic, suffered the loss of its [Queen](/wiki/Queen/Legends "Queen/Legends") [Silara Panteer](/wiki/Silara_Panteer "Silara Panteer") and her son [Gaul Panteer](/wiki/Gaul_Panteer "Gaul Panteer"), Alderaan's Senator, not long after the Senator declared Alderaan's independence following the Treaty of Coruscant. The death of the Panteers led to a crisis of succession that gave way to a three-way [civil war](/wiki/Alderaan_Civil_War "Alderaan Civil War") as the formerly exiled [House Thul](/wiki/House_of_Thul "House of Thul") returned with Imperial backing and General [Bouris Ulgo](/wiki/Bouris_Ulgo "Bouris Ulgo") declared himself king before wiping out the Panteers. Houses Thul and [Ulgo](/wiki/House_Ulgo "House Ulgo") are opposed by the Republic-allied [House Organa](/wiki/House_of_Organa/Legends "House of Organa/Legends"), and they all vie for supremacy as the minor houses ally themselves with the various factions. To make matters worse, amid the political conflict, hives of the insectoid [Killik](/wiki/Killik/Legends "Killik/Legends") species have awoken across Alderaan and are wreaking havoc.

On Alderaan, the Jedi Consular searches for Master [Sidonie Garen](/wiki/Sidonie_Garen "Sidonie Garen"), who was tasked with arranging a peace conference between the houses before she became infected with the Dark Plague. Upon discovering that Alderaanian law barred the Consular from attending, the Jedi allied with the lesser [House Teral](/wiki/House_Teral "House Teral") and became their advocate in order to attend the conference, aiding them against House Rist and securing an alliance with House Organa. At the conference, Garen's madness led her to try and sabotage the proceedings to incite war, but the Consular was able to restore order and end Garen's plans.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

The Knight arrives on Alderaan in search of the Jedi's former Master Orgus Din, who had also vanished while securing the [Death Mark laser](/wiki/Death_Mark_laser "Death Mark laser")—an orbital satellite meant to end the civil war by strategic assassination. With the help of a Republic scientist named [Aleyna Hark](/wiki/Aleyna_Hark "Aleyna Hark"), the Knight is able to locate Din and rescue him from the remains of the Death Mark research facility, only to find that Hark is a spy in the service of Angral's apprentice [Nefarid](/wiki/Nefarid "Nefarid")—and Hark is marking targets for Nefarid to kill with the Death Mark. After preventing Hark from killing [Duke](/wiki/Duke/Legends "Duke/Legends") [Horis Thul](/wiki/Horis_Thul "Horis Thul"), the Knight tracks down and defeats Nefarid, but at the same time, Master Din is killed during an [attempt](/wiki/Mission_to_the_Oppressor "Mission to the Oppressor") to infiltrate Darth Angral's ship.

With the Great Hunt drawing to a close, the hunter's next target is on Alderaan: [Duke](/wiki/Duke/Legends "Duke/Legends") [Corwin](/wiki/Corwin "Corwin"), the Durasteel Duke. The hunter seeks out Corwin's last known location—the noble family [House Girard](/wiki/House_Girard "House Girard")—and is recruited by Corwin's cousin, Baron [Zacar Girard](/wiki/Zacar_Girard "Zacar Girard"), to act as Girard's advocate in exchange for aid in the search. Tracking down the duke by tracing coded messages left in museum relics, the hunter pursues Corwin to [House Rist](/wiki/House_Rist_(estate) "House Rist (estate)") but arrives only to find that Corwin had already escaped to House Organa's protection. The hunter continues the pursuit nonetheless, but finds that the Duke is in fact dead and is being impersonated by his sister [Muriel](/wiki/Muriel_Corwin "Muriel Corwin") for the sake of a treaty. The hunter turns in the duke's corpse, successfully earning a place in the final round of the Great Hunt.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

Governor Chornarov's corruption attracts the attention of the Republic, which begins an investigation into his actions; however, when the Republic is prepared to arrest him, the governor makes his move. Broadcasting live on the Holonet, Chornarov declares Cademimu's independence from the Republic, and his [Cademiman Guard](/wiki/Cademiman_Guard "Cademiman Guard")—many of whom are former members of the Mantellian Separatist Movement—institute martial law on the planet. Cademimu is incredibly valuable to the Republic war effort, as it is the site of missile depots that supply Republic forces along the entire [Celanon Spur](/wiki/Celanon_Spur/Legends "Celanon Spur/Legends") trade route. Chornarov's actions draw the attention of both the Republic and the Empire, and both groups dispatch strike teams to the planet in order to take back control of the planet's missile depots and thereby allow a naval fleet to enter the system. Chornarov's subordinate General [Ortol](/wiki/Ortol "Ortol"), the leader of the Guard, is killed during the fighting, and the planet falls to one of the galactic powers.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

As the galaxy approaches war, the Republic forms a new squadron known as the [Coruscant Aegis](/wiki/Coruscant_Aegis "Coruscant Aegis") that sees service during both the Cold War and the Galactic War. The Coruscant Aegis [rescues](/wiki/Operation_Midnight_Freedom "Operation Midnight Freedom") a Republic transport in the [Fondor system](/wiki/Fondor_system/Legends "Fondor system/Legends"), [defends](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Syvris_system "Battle of the Syvris system") the personnel of a SIS listening post in the [Syvris system](/wiki/Syvris_system/Legends "Syvris system/Legends") when they are forced to evacuate, and [destroys](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Llanic_system "Battle of the Llanic system") an Imperial space station in the [Llanic system](/wiki/Llanic_system/Legends "Llanic system/Legends") that was developing a poison known as [Ziroxin-12](/wiki/Ziroxin-12/Legends "Ziroxin-12/Legends"). When an Imperial staging point is discovered in the [Balosar system](/wiki/Balosar_system/Legends "Balosar system/Legends"), the Republic sends the Coruscant Aegis to [destroy](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Balosar_system "Battle of the Balosar system") the space station, and they also [defeat](/wiki/Battle_of_Javaal "Battle of Javaal") the Empire's [Razor Shyracks](/wiki/Razor_Shyracks "Razor Shyracks") squadron and their leader, the Sith Lord [Kestas Rone](/wiki/Kestas_Rone "Kestas Rone"), over the planet [Javaal](/wiki/Javaal "Javaal"). In the [Archenar system](/wiki/Archenar_system/Legends "Archenar system/Legends"), the Aegis [eliminates](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Archenar_asteroid_field "Battle of the Archenar asteroid field") a group of Imperial fighters that has been preying on Republic supply transports in Hutt Space, and also [spearhead an assault](/wiki/Battle_of_Makem_Te_(Cold_War) "Battle of Makem Te (Cold War)") on the damaged warship [*Overlord*](/wiki/Overlord_(warship) "Overlord (warship)") over [Makem Te](/wiki/Makem_Te/Legends "Makem Te/Legends") when its commander, Moff [Jocend](/wiki/Jocend "Jocend") is forced to retreat there after a failed attack on Republic borders. Just before open war, the squadron [defends](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Pakuuni_system "Battle of the Pakuuni system") a neutral space station from Imperial attack in the [Pakuuni system](/wiki/Pakuuni_system/Legends "Pakuuni system/Legends"), foiling the Empire's efforts to blame the Republic. In the ice rings of [Kovor](/wiki/Kovor "Kovor"), the Aegis [defeats](/wiki/Battle_above_Kovor "Battle above Kovor") an Imperial force led by the pilot [Tervor Jheran](/wiki/Tervor_Jheran "Tervor Jheran") when Jheran attacked a Republic squadron and attempted to frame them for breaking the Treaty. The squadron also destroys the [Rancor's Claw](/wiki/Rancor%27s_Claw "Rancor's Claw") squadron in a [dogfight](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Drexel_system "Battle of the Drexel system") amid the asteroids of the [Drexel system](/wiki/Drexel_system/Legends "Drexel system/Legends") during the final days of the Cold War.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

Around the same time, the Empire forms the elite [Empire's Fury](/wiki/Empire%27s_Fury "Empire's Fury") squadron, which sees action across the galaxy. One of the squadron's first missions is the [destruction](/wiki/Attack_on_the_Hutt_Cartel_listening_post "Attack on the Hutt Cartel listening post") of a Republic listening post in Hutt Space, and the Empire's Fury also emerges victorious when they [engage](/wiki/Battle_above_Saleucami "Battle above Saleucami") the Republic's [Solar Thrantas](/wiki/Solar_Thrantas "Solar Thrantas") squadron and its Jedi leader, [Nezhel "Sunsport" Othren](/wiki/Nezhel_Othren "Nezhel Othren"), over the planet [Saleucami](/wiki/Saleucami/Legends "Saleucami/Legends"). When a Republic fighter wing is sighted over the Imperial [agriworld](/wiki/Agriworld/Legends "Agriworld/Legends") [Nez Peron](/wiki/Nez_Peron/Legends "Nez Peron/Legends"), the Empire's Fury is deployed to [wipe out](/wiki/Battle_of_Nez_Peron "Battle of Nez Peron") the starfighters for entering Imperial space, and the squadron also leads the [assault](/wiki/Battle_of_Sarapin_Four "Battle of Sarapin Four") on the Republic warship *[Enkindle](/wiki/Enkindle "Enkindle")* over [Sarapin Four](/wiki/Sarapin_Four "Sarapin Four") after the *Enkindle* is damaged in a confrontation with the Imperial dreadnought *[Tears of Taris](/wiki/Tears_of_Taris "Tears of Taris")*. The Empire's Fury also [rescues](/wiki/Operation_Silent_Roar "Operation Silent Roar") Imperial Intelligence agents who are fleeing Republic forces in the [Jabiim system](/wiki/Jabiim_system/Legends "Jabiim system/Legends"). The Empire's Fury squadron sees action against the Republic-sympathizing [Ezran pirates](/wiki/Ezran_pirates "Ezran pirates") in the [Ezran system](/wiki/Ezran_system/Legends "Ezran system/Legends") when the Empire learns that the pirates are sheltering Republic operatives, prompting the Empire's Fury to [wipe out](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Ezran_system "Battle of the Ezran system") the pirates. When Major [Boro Fareed](/wiki/Boro_Fareed "Boro Fareed") agrees to defect to the Empire, the Empire's Fury is sent to [rescue](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Taspan_system "Battle of the Taspan system") his shuttle from Republic forces in the [Taspan system](/wiki/Taspan_system "Taspan system") and escorts the defector to safety. When Republic forces [attack](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Skaross_system "Battle of the Skaross system") an Imperial manufacturing station in the [Skaross system](/wiki/Skaross_system/Legends "Skaross system/Legends") in violation of the ceasefire, the Empire's Fury wipes out the bombers and saves the station from the rogue Republic attackers. The Empire's Fury [wipes out](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Polith_system "Battle of the Polith system") Republic-sponsored pirates who are setting up a minefield in the [Polith system](/wiki/Polith_system "Polith system"), destroys the elite [Sullustan](/wiki/Sullustan/Legends "Sullustan/Legends") bomber squadron known as the [Ash Angels](/wiki/Ash_Angels "Ash Angels") when they [go rogue and attack](/wiki/Battle_of_Sululluub "Battle of Sululluub") Imperial forces in the Outer Rim, and [wipe out](/wiki/Battle_of_Mugaar "Battle of Mugaar") a Republic border patrol that the Empire lures away from Republic space into the ice rings of the planet [Mugaar](/wiki/Mugaar/Legends "Mugaar/Legends").[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

The Republic does not have to wait long for Darth Angral's next move—using a tracking device planted by Din before his death, the Republic locates Angral's warship in the [Uphrades system](/wiki/Uphrades_system/Legends "Uphrades system/Legends"), but when the Knight arrives there, the fertile [agriworld](/wiki/Agriworld/Legends "Agriworld/Legends") [Uphrades](/wiki/Uphrades "Uphrades") has been utterly devastated by some kind of combination of the stolen superweapons. The Knight and company rescue the stricken medical frigate *[Daybreaker](/wiki/Daybreaker "Daybreaker")* from an Imperial attack and learn from the survivors that Angral has combined the stolen superweapons into a single ship-mounted weapon: the Desolator. Having tested the Desolator on Uphrades, Angral sets his sights on Tython itself, and the Knight's crew arrives in the Tython system as the Desolator recharges for an attack. Slipping aboard the *Oppressor*, the Knight and Carsen disable the Desolator's reactors before facing Angral himself on the ship's bridge. However, the Emperor seizes control of Carsen briefly and orders Angral to kill the Knight. Angral falls in battle to the Knight and Carsen, but the Emperor fully possesses Carsen and attacks the Knight with Angral's fallen weapon. As the *Oppressor* begins to disintegrate under Jedi bombing runs, the Knight helps Carsen purge herself of the Emperor's influence, and the two escape the doomed warship. In the aftermath of the [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_the_Oppressor "Battle of the Oppressor"), Carsen is elevated to the rank of Jedi Knight, and Din's former student is named "the Hero of Tython."[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

Studying what they know about Vivicar, the Council determines that Vivicar is likely Parkanas Tark himself, out for revenge against those who left him on Malachor—and Yuon Par something more: Malachor III was the resting place of [Terrak Morrhage](/wiki/Terrak_Morrhage "Terrak Morrhage"), the original creator of the dark plague. Using the connection forged by the plague between herself and Tark, Par attempts to track Vivicar's location, and she is successful despite a brief possession by Vivicar. The Consular travels to Vivicar's location, a [ship](/wiki/Vivicar%27s_ship "Vivicar's ship") drifting in deep space filled with brainwashed Republic soldiers, and confronts the Sith Lord. However, Tark is revealed to be nothing more than a vessel for the spirit of Terrak Morrhage, which had been awoken by the Padawans on their expedition, and despite his being defeated in a duel with the Consular, Morrhage reveals that he is infecting hundreds more Jedi Masters with each passing moment. Should Vivicar die, the infected would die as well, so the Consular instead uses the shielding technique on Vivicar, freeing Tark and forcing a weakened Morrhage to vanish while also freeing the infected. In the aftermath, Tark goes into self-imposed exile on Tython, and the Consular is granted the rank of Jedi Master and the title of [Barsen'thor](/wiki/Barsen%27thor "Barsen'thor"), or Warden of the Order.

With the Corwin bounty finished, the hunter is contacted by former Grand Champion [Hedarr Soongh](/wiki/Hedarr_Soongh "Hedarr Soongh"), who warns the hunter that Tarro Blood's allies are gathering on Nar Shaddaa to plan an attack. Heeding the advice, the hunter disrupts Blood's allies' plans, but Soongh is killed in the chaos.
