:   ―Daimon Schubert[[238]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Update_2.0-238)

**Game Update 2.0: Scum and Villainy** went live on the Public Test Server on [February 20](/wiki/February_20 "February 20"), 2013,[[239]](#cite_note-Update_2.0_PTS-239) and was released to the public on April 9 in order to coincide with the release of *Rise of the Hutt Cartel* for players who have pre-ordered the expansion. With the release of the update, Planetary Commendations have been consolidated into one type, and Elder Game Commendations have been reworked in order to reduce confusion. New Basic Commendations are earned through Level 51+ activities, while Elite Commendations are earned from Level 55 Flashpoints and Ultimate Commendations from Level 55 Operations. Additional items, included Sith armor inspired by the *Deceived* trailer, have been added to the Cartel Market, and players in guilds now gain a 5% experience gain bonus. Priority Transport Terminals have also been added to both factions' fleets, allowing easier access to the daily mission areas.[[238]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Update_2.0-238)

Furthermore, Game Update 2.0 introduces the new Operation Scum and Villainy, where players travel to the new planet of Darvannis. All Flashpoints and Operations now reward players with improved gear, and Level 55 players can now participate in Hard Mode versions for Flashpoints Hammer Station, Athiss, Mandalorian Raiders, and Cademimu as well as Nightmare mode for Terror From Beyond. Another major feature is the addition of the Legacy Achievements system, which introduces over 1,900 Achievements that players can earn on any character in their Legacy. Achievements can grant rewards, including Cartel Coins and new titles. However, some features included in the update, such as the increase in level cap to 55 and the addition of [macrobinoculars](/wiki/Macrobinoculars/Legends "Macrobinoculars/Legends") and [subterranean seeker droids](/wiki/Seeker_Droid "Seeker Droid"), are reserved for players who have purchased *Rise of the Hutt Cartel*.[[238]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Update_2.0-238)

With the release of Update 2.0, the combat system for all classes has been overhauled. The Alacrity stat has been altered to increase the activation speed of abilities and resource regeneration, which also has the effect of speeding up combat animations. Shields and the Accuracy stat have also been altered, increasing their importance and usefulness to many classes. The skill trees for all classes and advanced classes underwent significant changes, with more than half of the abilities and skills having been either replaced or altered. In the second week after the release of Update 2.0, a series of Developer Blogs were posted on the game's official site in order to give players more information on the changes for each class.[[240]](#cite_note-Class_Changes-240)

#### Game Update 2.1: Customization

 [![Update 2](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/Update_2.1.png/revision/latest?cb=20130720181442) [![Update 2](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/Update_2.1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20130720181442)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/Update_2.1.png/revision/latest?cb=20130720181442) 

Update 2.1: Customization

 

:   "*We are thrilled to release Game Update 2.1: Customization today. This update introduces many highly requested and anticipated features to* Star Wars*: The Old Republic. As the name indicates, Game Update 2.1 is all about giving players the freedom to customize their characters to fully immerse themselves in their personal* Star Wars *saga.*"
:   ―Cory Butler[[34]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Update_2.1-34)

**Game Update 2.1: Customization** was first announced on April 26 in a video that previewed the addition of the Cathar as a playable species.[[241]](#cite_note-Cathar_Preview_Video-241) The April edition of The Old Republic Insider, released the same day, gave further information on the update, announcing the addition of the Appearance Designer Kiosk as well as upcoming Cartel Market items.[[197]](#cite_note-Insider_April-197) The Kiosk allows players to completely recreate their character's appearances in exchange for Cartel Coins, and the addition of Dye Modules allows players to change the colors of any crafted gear above Level 15. The update was released on [May 14](/wiki/May_14 "May 14"), and included the addition of the Collections Interface, which allows players to unlock Cartel Market items for their entire account at a discount price.[[34]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Update_2.1-34) Additionally, with the release of Update 2.1 players are now able to purchase a variety of Convenience Services, including Character Rename, Legacy Rename, and Guild Rename, in the Cartel Market.[[37]](#cite_note-Game_Update_2.1:_Customization-37)

Game Update 2.1 was originally announced as "Dance of the Hutts" as part of an April Fool's joke on *The Old Republic*'s official site. The proposed update would have featured a new PvP area entitled "Toborro's Shakedown" in which players would hold dance-offs against each other, and also a rideable Hutt mount known as the "Huttese Transporter."[[242]](#cite_note-Update_2.1_Fake-242)

#### Game Update 2.2: Operation Nightmare

 [![Update 2](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fa/Update_2.2.png/revision/latest?cb=20130720191650) [![Update 2](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fa/Update_2.2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20130720191650)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fa/Update_2.2.png/revision/latest?cb=20130720191650) 

Update 2.2: Operation Nightmare

 

:   "*Put your guild's coordination and skill to the ultimate test as you conquer twelve nightmarish bosses on the planets of Asation and Darvannis in two newly upgraded Level 55 Nightmare Mode Operations coming soon in Game Update 2.2: Operation Nightmare. Fight for a chance to earn a brand new set of Kell Dragon gear, the most powerful PvE gear available, along with two new stunning vehicles.*"
:   ―Announcement for Update 2.2[[243]](#cite_note-Update_2.2_Announcement-243)

**Game Update 2.2: Operation Nightmare** was first announced on [May 24](/wiki/May_24 "May 24") during Bruce Maclean's "Summer of SWTOR" announcement,[[244]](#cite_note-Summer_of_SWTOR-244) and it was released in two parts. The first, Update 2.2, added a Nightmare Mode for Terror From Beyond, as well as new guild bonuses, two new vehicles, and the Kell Dragon PvE gear set. Underworld Gear crafting was also added in the first part, and the second part—Update 2.2.2—added a Nightmare Mode to Scum and Villainy.[[243]](#cite_note-Update_2.2_Announcement-243) Update 2.2 was released on [June 12](/wiki/June_12 "June 12"),[[245]](#cite_note-Update_2.2-245) though Update 2.2.2 was not released until July 10.[[246]](#cite_note-Update_2.2.2_Live-246)

#### Game Update 2.3: Titans of Industry

 [![Update 2](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/Update_2.3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130807141930) [![Update 2](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/Update_2.3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20130807141930)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/31/Update_2.3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130807141930) 

Update 2.3: Titans of Industry

 

:   "***Titans of Industry** is a new story arc encompassing two new Flashpoints at level 55: **Czerka Corporate Labs** and **Czerka Core Meltdown**. These Flashpoints can be accessed by traveling to a small daily mission area, CZ-198 via your ship or the Priority Transport Terminal.*"
:   ―Bruce Maclean[[247]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Update_2.3-247)

**Game Update 2.3: Titans of Industry** is a Czerka-themed update that was first announced during Bruce Maclean's "Summer of SWTOR" announcement on May 24[[244]](#cite_note-Summer_of_SWTOR-244) and released on [August 6](/wiki/August_6 "August 6").[[247]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Update_2.3-247) The update went live on the Public Test Server on [June 28](/wiki/June_28 "June 28"), when it was announced that the update would be centered around three main additions: a new Level 55 daily mission area and two new Flashpoints. The mission area is the moon of CZ-198, which is the site of a major Czerka Corporation [facility](/wiki/Czerka_facility_(CZ-198) "Czerka facility (CZ-198)") that has recently entered an emergency lockdown, while the Flashpoint: Czerka Corporate Labs and Flashpoint: Czerka Core Meltdown deal with various crises at the facility.[[248]](#cite_note-Update_2.3_PTS-248) In the July edition of The Old Republic Insider, it was revealed that Update 2.3 would include a new Ewok companion named Treek that would be available for all classes,[[198]](#cite_note-Insider_July-198) and on July 5 the new recurring Bounty Contract Week was announced, as was the addition of the Cartel Bazaar areas to both factions' fleets.[[249]](#cite_note-Bounty_Contract_Week-249)

With the release of Game Update 2.3, [Tauntaun](/wiki/Tauntaun/Legends "Tauntaun/Legends") Mounts are added to the game, and three new organizations—the Adjudicators, the Ordnance Acquisition Corps, and the Bounty Brokers Association—are added to the Reputation system.[[247]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Update_2.3-247) Update 2.3 also saw a reworking of the game's visuals with new palette graphics, with every planet's environment receiving alterations in their color schemes to better reflect the planet and to create contrast between different regions.[[250]](#cite_note-Developer_Update:_Color_Palette_Upgrade-250) The Czerka storyline of Titans of Industry was planned as far back as the 2012 leak, which included the introductory conversations for the update's storyline.

#### Game Update 2.4: The Dread War

 [![Update 2](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/Update_2.4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130914053908) [![Update 2](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/Update_2.4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20130914053908)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/Update_2.4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130914053908) 

Update 2.4: The Dread War

 

:   "*This is our biggest Game Update since 2.0 and includes a story mission area with new missions on a new moon, two entirely new Operations, all new 4v4 Warzone gameplay and Arenas, class balance changes, three new sets of gear comprising some of the most powerful equipment in the galaxy, and new vehicles and mount rewards!*"
:   ―Bruce Maclean[[30]](#cite_note-The_Search_for_Oricon-30)

**Game Update 2.4: The Dread War**, promoted as the "Last Chapter in the Dread Masters Saga," was first mentioned on July 16 when developers confirmed a variety of features that would be introduced in the update,[[244]](#cite_note-Summer_of_SWTOR-244) and the update went live on the Public Test Server a month later on August 16,[[251]](#cite_note-Update_2.4_PTS-251) followed by the update's official release on [October 1](/wiki/October_1 "October 1").[[252]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Update_2.4-252) In a press release on September 12, BioWare announced that Update 2.4 would be released on October 1. Update 2.4 centers on the final confrontation with the Dread Masters, who have retreated to their Dread Fortress on the moon of Oricon, and the two new Operations: Dread Fortress and Dread Palace.[[253]](#cite_note-Update_2.4_Announcement-253) Oricon is a new story mission area with a world arc for each faction and additional Level 55 Daily Missions, and two Reputation organizations for Oricon have been added: the Republic's Strike Team Oricon and the Empire's Dread Executioners.[[110]](#cite_note-Update_2.4_Patch_Notes-110)

Update 2.4 also introduces the new Warzone Arenas, which are Last Team Standing Warzones that pit teams of 4 players against each other in battles to eliminate the opposing team, with a best of three rounds per match. The first three "Arenas of Death," as the Warzones are called in-game, are on Corellia, Tatooine, and an Orbital Station. Update 2.4 also sees the removal of 8v8 Ranked Warzones, as the limited number of eight-player groups willing and able to play in those matches made 8v8 Ranked matches very rare. Warzone Arenas are restricted to subscribers as of Update 2.4, though a removal of this restriction and an additional Warzone Arena map are planned.[[95]](#cite_note-Developer_Update:_Warzone_Arena-95) Three additional gear sets and a number of new vehicle and mounts are added in the update, and the update included a variety of minor changes to the various advanced classes in order to better balance gameplay.[[110]](#cite_note-Update_2.4_Patch_Notes-110)

#### Game Update 2.5: Galactic Starfighter Subscriber Early Access

 [![Update 2](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/Update_2.5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140223063609) [![Update 2](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/Update_2.5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20140223063609)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d2/Update_2.5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140223063609) 

Update 2.5: *Galactic Starfighter* Early Access

 

:   "*The no-longer-super-secret space project has been revealed at last! We are working hard to bring you the Galactic Starfighter™ free Digital Expansion in February, but on December 3rd we are planning to open it up to Subscribers with Game Update 2.5: Galactic Starfighter Subscriber Early Access. Also in Game Update 2.5 we'll have continued class balance updates and an all new PvP Warzone Arena, the Makeb Mesa Arena.*"
:   ―Bruce Maclean[[202]](#cite_note-Holiday_Update-202)

**Game Update 2.5: Galactic Starfighter Subscriber Early Access** was first announced in a blog update about the holiday plans for *The Old Republic* on October 18, 2013 with a release date of [December 3](/wiki/December_3 "December 3"). The bulk of the update focused on the addition of the Digital Expansion *Galactic Starfighter*, which was made available to subscribers. Game Update 2.5 also included class balance changes and the Makeb Mesa PvP Warzone Arena.[[202]](#cite_note-Holiday_Update-202) Two maps for the Galactic Starfighter Domination game mode were made available—Lost Shipyards and Kuat Mesas—and a new Reputation organization, The Hyland Organization for Rakghoul Neutralization (T.H.O.R.N.) was added.[[111]](#cite_note-Update_2.5_Patch_Notes-111)

#### Game Update 2.6: Galactic Starfighter

 [![Game Update 2](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Update_2.6.png/revision/latest?cb=20140223064551) [![Game Update 2](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Update_2.6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20140223064551)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Update_2.6.png/revision/latest?cb=20140223064551) 

Game Update 2.6: Galactic Starfighter

 

:   "*For those of you who haven't yet experienced Galactic Starfighter, now is the perfect time. Starting today, anyone with an account can log into the game and immediately access all that Galactic Starfighter has to offer. We have many new additions and improvements to the game including a brand new role in the Bomber and a new gameplay mode, Team Death Match!*"
:   ―Jack Wood[[254]](#cite_note-Game_Update_2.6_Blog-254)

**Game Update 2.6: Galactic Starfighter** was announced in a Developer Tracker post on [January 2](/wiki/January_2 "January 2"), 2014, and was the official launch of *Galactic Starfighter* on [February 4](/wiki/February_4 "February 4"), 2014. The update added a number of new content elements, including the gunship for Free-to-Play players, a new Gunship variant, and two new Bomber variants for a total of six new ships. A DPS boost was implemented for Operatives and Scoundrels, and a number of combat modifications were added for Mercenaries, Commandos, Sorcerers, and Sages.[[255]](#cite_note-DevTracker2.6-255) The update went live on the Public Test Server on January 10, including a new Tactical Flashpoint: Kuat Drive Yards that is role-neutral, the Team Deathmatch mode for *Galactic Starfighter*, and a number of new improvements for the expansion.[[256]](#cite_note-Update_2.6_PTS-256)

#### Game Update 2.7: Invasion

 [![Game Update 2](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Update_2.7.png/revision/latest?cb=20140708162740) [![Game Update 2](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Update_2.7.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20140708162740)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6c/Update_2.7.png/revision/latest?cb=20140708162740) 

Game Update 2.7: Invasion

 

:   "*A new story arc begins with Forged Alliances: Part I, which includes two new level 55 Tactical Flashpoints: Assault on Tython and Korriban Incursion. This epic new storyline for* Star Wars*™: The Old Republic™ introduces two major characters – Theron Shan and Lana Beniko. The three part story will continue to be expanded throughout the year culminating in an incredible finale.*"
:   ―Bruce Maclean[[257]](#cite_note-Game_Update_2.7-257)

**Game Update 2.7: Invasion**[[258]](#cite_note-Invasion_Name-258) was first announced on [February 3](/wiki/February_3 "February 3"), 2014 with an intended release date of [April 8](/wiki/April_8 "April 8"),[[70]](#cite_note-Road_Map_2014-70) and went live on the Public Test Server at the end of February, at which time the update's name was announced.[[258]](#cite_note-Invasion_Name-258) The update included two new Tactical Flashpoints—Assault on Tython and Korriban Incursion—that are the start of "Forged Alliances,"[[73]](#cite_note-Update_2.7_PTS-73) a year-long storyline that sees the Republic and the Empire confront one another directly.[[70]](#cite_note-Road_Map_2014-70) Other content included a Nightmare Mode for the Dread Fortress Operation, a new tier of gear,[[70]](#cite_note-Road_Map_2014-70) the new Domination map Denon Exosphere for *Galactic Starfighter*, and a new Huttball Warzone, Quesh Huttball Pit. The update also featured combat changes to a majority of the sixteen advanced classes.[[73]](#cite_note-Update_2.7_PTS-73)

#### Game Update 2.8: Spoils of War

 [![Game Update 2](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/29/Update_2.8.png/revision/latest?cb=20140708151737) [![Game Update 2](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/29/Update_2.8.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20140708151737)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/29/Update_2.8.png/revision/latest?cb=20140708151737) 

Game Update 2.8: Spoils of War

 

:   "*With this update we hope to give you plenty of different activities to while away your summer. We're kicking things off with some increased Galactic Starfighter rewards – you'll get double Fleet Requisition & Credits for completing GSF matches. This will last 3 weeks until 2.8.1 hits, at which time we'll switch our focus over to Warzones and double your Commendations & Credits for completing those matches.*"
:   ―Andrew Horwitz[[259]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Update_2.8-259)

**Game Update 2.8: Spoils of War** was first announced on February 3, 2014 with an intended release date of [June 10](/wiki/June_10 "June 10"), and was touted as the largest game update since the game launched. As of February, known content for the update included a Nightmare Mode of the Dread Palace Operation, and new ships and a new Ship Role for *Galactic Starfighter*.[[70]](#cite_note-Road_Map_2014-70) However, the expansion's release was later postponed until June 28 to give the developers more time to complete the stronghold content. Subscriber Early Access for *Galactic Strongholds* was planned to be launched with Update 2.8, but was delayed until Update 2.9's release on [August 19](/wiki/August_19 "August 19").[[260]](#cite_note-2.8_Delayed-260) Update 2.8 first went live on the Public Test Server on [May 1](/wiki/May_1 "May 1").[[261]](#cite_note-Update_2.8_PTS-261) The update's name was revealed on May 14, when the Festival of Splender in-game event was also announced along with a new group-finder for Story Mode Operations, and a new variant for the Gunship and the Bomber classes.[[262]](#cite_note-Game_Update_2.8:_Spoils_of_War-262) Game Update 2.8 was accompanied by three weeks of double Fleet Requisition and credit rewards for completing *Galactic Starfighter* matches, after which the rewards shifted to Warzones. The Rakghoul Resurgence event was supposedly discontinued, though other events such as a July 4 Double XP Weekend, the Relics of the Gree, and Bounty Contract Week returned in the summer.[[259]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Update_2.8-259) The update also introduced NPC models for a number of alien species, including [Klatooinians](/wiki/Klatooinian/Legends "Klatooinian/Legends"), [Snivvians](/wiki/Snivvian/Legends "Snivvian/Legends"), [Ishi Tib](/wiki/Ishi_Tib/Legends "Ishi Tib/Legends"), and [Aqualish](/wiki/Aqualish/Legends "Aqualish/Legends").[[263]](#cite_note-Developer_Update:_Spoils_of_War-263)

#### Game Update 2.9: Galactic Strongholds Early Access

 [![Game Update 2](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Update_2.9.png/revision/latest?cb=20140907212705) [![Game Update 2](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Update_2.9.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20140907212705)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cc/Update_2.9.png/revision/latest?cb=20140907212705) 

Game Update 2.9: Galactic Strongholds Early Access

 

:   "*The introduction of Galactic Strongholds brings you a multitude of new features that have never been seen before in* Star Wars*™: The Old Republic™! Galactic Strongholds fulfills your dreams of owning your own home in the* Star Wars*™ universe, establishing your own Guild Headquarters in one of our four Stronghold locations, or conquering the galaxy in a formidable Guild Flagship!*"
:   ―Jack Wood[[114]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Galactic_Strongholds_Early_Access-114)

**Game Update 2.9: Galactic Strongholds Early Access** was first announced on [April 23](/wiki/April_23 "April 23"), 2014 as the launch date for Subscriber Early Access to the new *Galactic Strongholds* Digital Expansion. The expansion's launch was originally planned for June, but delayed so the team could add additional features.[[264]](#cite_note-Producer_Letter:_Galactic_Strongholds-264) It was released on [August 19](/wiki/August_19 "August 19"), 2014, and featured the launch of both *Galactic Strongholds* and the Depths of Manaan Tactical Flashpoint, which continues the Forged Alliances storyline.[[114]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Galactic_Strongholds_Early_Access-114) The Flashpoint is accessible via the new "planet" of Manaan, which appears on the galaxy map but currently only features a vendor and the Flashpoint entrance.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24) Ranked Arena Season 2 also came to an end with Update 2.9, and the new GSI Satellite Support Service was launched on Makeb, boosting armor ratings and giving additional bonuses.[[113]](#cite_note-Update_2.9_Patch_Notes-113)

#### Game Update 2.10: Forged Alliances

 [![Game Update 2](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c4/Update_2.10.png/revision/latest?cb=20150321185510) [![Game Update 2](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c4/Update_2.10.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20150321185510)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c4/Update_2.10.png/revision/latest?cb=20150321185510) 

Game Update 2.10: Forged Alliances

 

:   "*Don't miss out on the epic finale to the 'Forged Alliances' storyline with the release of the new Legacy of the Rakata Flashpoint, now live! Discover the mysteries of the historic planet of Rakata Prime, a tropical world largely covered in oceans, home to the Rakata species and also referred to as the 'Unknown World.'*"
:   ―Game Update 2.10 announcement[[265]](#cite_note-Rakata_Flashpoint-265)

**Game Update 2.10: Forged Alliances** was first mentioned in the exclusive content given to fans who attended the Cantina Tour at August's Gamescom 2014,[[266]](#cite_note-Dulfy_Gamescon_2014-266) and the Cantina Tour at PAX Prime 2014 a few weeks later set the update's release date as [September 9](/wiki/September_9 "September 9").[[267]](#cite_note-Dulfy_PAX_2014-267) The finale of the "Forged Alliances" storyline, Update 2.10 introduces the new Tactical Flashpoint: Legacy of the Rakata, which sees players pursue Colonel Darok and Darth Arkous to Rakata Prime. The update also featured a significant amount of class combat changes that were kept back from Update 2.9 due to technical reasons. Ranked Warzone Arena Season 3 began with the update, as did the September instance of the Bounty Contract Week event.[[268]](#cite_note-Update_2.10_Patch_Notes-268)

#### Game Update 3.0: Shadow of Revan Early Access

 [![Game Update 3](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Shadow_of_Revan_art.png/revision/latest?cb=20141209031659) [![Game Update 3](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Shadow_of_Revan_art.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20141209031659)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Shadow_of_Revan_art.png/revision/latest?cb=20141209031659) 

Game Update 3.0: Shadow of Revan Early Access

 

:   "*Of course, we haven't left out the usual accoutrements you'd expect from an expansion of this magnitude. The first thing you'll notice when you log into the game is the new Disciplines system. This has replaced the old Skill Trees system in favor of a more streamlined and user friendly system that allows you to experience the core of your character's Class very early on in the game. From there, the game opens up into the Forged Alliances prelude, where you are able to play single-player versions of the Forged Alliances Flashpoints on Tython, Korriban, Manaan, & Rakata Prime.*"
:   ―Andrew Horwitz[[269]](#cite_note-Shadow_Welcome-269)

**Game Update 3.0: Shadow of Revan Early Access** was first announced alongside *Shadow of Revan* on [October 6](/wiki/October_6 "October 6"), 2014, with an intended release date of [December 2](/wiki/December_2 "December 2") in order to coincide with the release of Early Access for *Shadow of Revan*. In addition to the Digital Expansion, which adds the two new worlds of Rishi and Yavin 4, the two new Flashpoints Blood Hunt and Battle of Rishi, and the new Operations Temple of Sacrifice and The Ravagers,[[14]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_Revan-14) Game Update 3.0 introduced the new Discipline system, which replaced the prior Skill Tree system for advanced class skills.[[39]](#cite_note-Disciplines-39) New content included solo versions and Hard Modes for the four Forged Alliances Flashpoints, a new level cap of 500 for Crew Skills, and the end of Ranked Arena Season 3, and the Bounty Contract Week also returned at the full launch of the expansion. Update 3.0 also saw the launch of a new visualization system called Effect Procs, which highlights hotbar buttons to show which abilities are "powered up" by active effects.[[102]](#cite_note-Update_3.0_Patch_Notes-102)

#### Game Update 3.1: Conflict on Rishi

 [![Game Update 3](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Update_3.1.png/revision/latest?cb=20150321185705) [![Game Update 3](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Update_3.1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20150321185705)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Update_3.1.png/revision/latest?cb=20150321185705) 

Game Update 3.1: Conflict on Rishi

 

:   "*Rally three of your most trusted allies and return to the dangerous pirate haven of Rishi to fight through Level 60 Hard Mode versions of the two newest story-driven Flashpoints, Blood Hunt and Battle of Rishi. Plus, compete for glory and new rewards in PvP Season 4 – all in Game Update 3.1: Conflict on Rishi!*"
:   ―Update 3.1 announcement[[270]](#cite_note-Conflict_Rishi-270)

**Game Update 3.1: Conflict on Rishi** was first announced in January 2015 with an intended release date of early February,[[91]](#cite_note-2015_PvP-91) and was released on [February 10](/wiki/February_10 "February 10"). The update's primary addition is Hard Mode versions of the Battle of Rishi and Blood Hunt Flashpoints from *Shadow of Revan*, and the start of Season 4 for the Ranked Warzones, which lasted roughly three months before ending with Game Update 3.2. The new Massassi Gear Set, two new walkers, and several decorations were added as rewards for the new Hard Mode Flashpoints.[[271]](#cite_note-Update_3.1-271)

#### Game Update 3.2: Rise of the Emperor

:   "*Unleashed from his sanctuary on Yavin 4, the former Sith Emperor has now struck the Imperial world of Ziost. Using his immense power in the dark side of the Force™, he has dominated the minds of the planet's Imperial troops--as well as an elite cadre of militaristic Jedi--and has set them against the populace, engaging in a bloody slaughter. Join with allies Lana Beniko and Theron Shan to stop the Emperor's terrifying assault in Game Update 3.2: Rise of the Emperor!*"
:   ―Update 3.2 description[[272]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Emperor-272)

 [![Game Update 3](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b1/Update_3.2.png/revision/latest?cb=20150811093022) [![Game Update 3](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b1/Update_3.2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20150811093022)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b1/Update_3.2.png/revision/latest?cb=20150811093022) 

Game Update 3.2: Rise of the Emperor

 

**Game Update 3.2: Rise of the Emperor** was first announced in January 2015,[[118]](#cite_note-Pax_South_Cantina_Tour-118) and was released on [April 28](/wiki/April_28 "April 28").[[35]](#cite_note-3.2_Livestream-35) PvP Season 4 ends with Game Update 3.2, and Season 5 launched without a preseason like previous iterations.[[91]](#cite_note-2015_PvP-91) The update's main focus is Ziost, a new Daily Area with a storyline that continues the events of *Shadow of Revan* and centers on the former Sith Emperor's actions after Yavin 4. The finale to the Ziost storyline was not made accessible upon the update's release; the endgame became available on May 4 as part of the celebration of Star Wars Day, and opens up the Daily Area version of Ziost. The update was preceded by a series of short stories released on the game's official website, introducing the Sixth Line and expanding on the stories of Theron Shan and Lana Beniko.[[272]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Emperor-272)

#### Game Update 3.3: Grand Togruta Celebration

 [![Game Update 3](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/Update_3.3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150811093831) [![Game Update 3](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/Update_3.3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20150811093831)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/Update_3.3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150811093831) 

Game Update 3.3: Grand Togruta Celebration

 

**Game Update 3.3: Grand Togruta Celebration** was first officially announced in a developer Livestream on [June 3](/wiki/June_3 "June 3"), 2015, and was released on [July 22](/wiki/July_22 "July 22"), 2015. It features the addition of the [Togruta](/wiki/Togruta/Legends "Togruta/Legends") as a playable species and a new Stronghold on Yavin 4.[[38]](#cite_note-3.3_Togruta_Celebration-38) The update also featured an extensive overhaul of the PvP gear system—removing Ranked Warzone Commendations, which were required to purchase the high-tier PvP gear and were much harder to earn. Existing Ranked Commendations were converted to standard Warzone Commendations, and the prices for both tiers of PvP gear were drastically reduced. Players also gained the ability to transfer Warzone Commendations between their characters, and the Commendations limit was raised from a maximum of a few thousand to 200,000. Additional improvements and tweaks to the PvP rewards and elements of warzones were included in the update.[[87]](#cite_note-Dulfy_3.3-87)

#### Game Update 4.0: Knights of the Fallen Empire

**Game Update 4.0: Knights of the Fallen Empire** was first mentioned on [June 12](/wiki/June_12 "June 12"), 2015,[[273]](#cite_note-EA-273) and was released on [October 20](/wiki/October_20 "October 20"), 2015. The update replaces the four primary stats Strength, Willpower, Cunning and Aim with a new single stat called Mastery. Flashpoints and Operations have been updated, with many new modes added for older Flashpoints and a new Flashpoint called "Star Fortress." Furthermore, subscribers now have the option to start their game at level 60. The primary addition to this update is the new *Knights of the Fallen Empire* storyline, available at level 60 (only for subscribers). *Knights of the Fallen Empire* continues from the events of *Rise of the Emperor*. The new storyline also adds new companions. A new planet, [Zakuul](/wiki/Zakuul "Zakuul"), is also available for all players.[[93]](#cite_note-Update_4.0-93)

#### Game Update 4.1: Anarchy in Paradise

**Game Update 4.1: Anarchy in Paradise** was released on [February 8](/wiki/February_8 "February 8"), [2016](/wiki/2016 "2016") and mainly added a new chapter for the *Knights of the Fallen Empire* storyline, featuring the mercenary [Firebrand](/wiki/Kaliyo_Djannis "Kaliyo Djannis"), along with the two new Alliance Alerts, "Arma Rasa" and "Little Boss." Crew Skills were also revisited.[[274]](#cite_note-Update_4.1-274)

#### Game Update 4.2: Disavowed

**Game Update 4.2: Disavowed** was released on [March 8](/wiki/March_8 "March 8"), 2016. The update added an eleventh chapter for the *Knights of the Fallen Empire* storyline, allowing the player to battle alongside [Major](/wiki/Major/Legends "Major/Legends") [Aric Jorgan](/wiki/Aric_Jorgan "Aric Jorgan"). The update also saw the return of the "Relics of the Gree" and "Bounty Contract Week" Events.[[275]](#cite_note-Update_4.2-275)

#### Game Update 4.3: Visions in the Dark

**Game Update 4.3: Visions in the Dark** was released on [April 5](/wiki/April_5 "April 5"), 2016 and added the twelfth chapter of the *Knights of the Fallen Empire* storyline. The chapter focuses on the confrontation between the player and [Emperor](/wiki/Emperor/Legends "Emperor/Legends") [Valkorion](/wiki/Tenebrae "Tenebrae"). The update started Ranked Warzone Arena Season 7 and added the new Warzone: Odessen Proving Grounds and the new Warzone Arena: Rishi Cove Arena. The update also allowed PVE and PVP players to play together, with the new gameplay option "Focus." The Bounty Contract Week Event also returned. Players were also able to now unlock additional Strongholds.[[276]](#cite_note-Update_4.3-276)

#### Game Update 4.4: Profit and Plunder

**Game Update 4.4: Profit and Plunder** was released on [May 3](/wiki/May_3 "May 3"), 2016 and added the thirteenth chapter of the *Knights of the Fallen Empire* storyline. The chapter focuses on the heist on the Emperor's secret treasury, the *[Gilded Star](/wiki/Gilded_Star "Gilded Star")*. The update also introduced the Eternal Championship, a tournament where players can face off against the galaxy's most notorious fighters.[[277]](#cite_note-Update_4.4-277)

#### Game Update 4.5: Mandalore's Revenge

**Game Update 4.5: Mandalore's Revenge** was released on [June 1](/wiki/June_1 "June 1"), 2016 and added the fourteenth chapter of the *Knights of the Fallen Empire* storyline. The chapter focuses on [Mandalorian forces](/wiki/Mandalorian_Trat%27ade "Mandalorian Trat'ade") [raiding](/wiki/Raid_on_Darvannis "Raid on Darvannis") an Eternal Empire [factory](/wiki/Darvannis_factory "Darvannis factory"), along with a new Alliance Alert: "Freedom Fight."[[278]](#cite_note-Update_4.5-278)

#### Game Update 4.6: The GEMINI Deception

**Game Update 4.6: The GEMINI Deception** was released on [June 28](/wiki/June_28 "June 28"), 2016. This update introduced the fifteenth chapter of the *Knights of the Fallen Empire* storyline, taking the Outlander into the heart of the Eternal Fleet's control systems. Players face off against the droid known as GEMINI, uncovering secrets about the fleet's design. The patch also introduced a galactic event in celebration of *The Old Republic*'s 5-year anniversary and new character perks.[[279]](#cite_note-Update_4.6-279)

#### Game Update 4.7: The Battle of Odessen

**Game Update 4.7: The Battle of Odessen** was released on [August 9](/wiki/August_9 "August 9"), 2016 and concluded the *Knights of the Fallen Empire* storyline with Chapter XVI. In this chapter, the Alliance launches a decisive battle against Arcann's forces on Odessen and a new Alliance Alert: "Shining in the Darkness." The update also added weapon tuning slots to high-end gear, fixed companion stance issues, and introduced a companion locator terminal to assist in regaining companions.[[280]](#cite_note-Update_4.7-280)

#### Game Update 5.0: Knights of the Eternal Throne

**Game Update 5.0: Knights of the Eternal Throne** (Early Access beginning [November 29](/wiki/November_29 "November 29"), 2016; full launch on [December 2](/wiki/December_2 "December 2"), 2016) continues the Alliance's conflict against the Eternal Empire with nine new chapters. The patch also raised the level cap from 65 to 70 and introduced the Galactic Command system and Uprisings—replayable 4-player flashpoint content.[[281]](#cite_note-Update_5.0-281)

#### Game Update 5.1: Defend the Throne

**Game Update 5.1: Defend the Throne** was released on [January 23](/wiki/January_23 "January 23"), 2017, adding Master Mode difficulty to all *Knights of the Fallen Empire* and *Knights of the Eternal Throne* chapters and introducing five new Uprisings.[[282]](#cite_note-Update_5.1-282)

#### Game Update 5.2: The War for Iokath

**Game Update 5.2: The War for Iokath** was released on [April 18](/wiki/April_18 "April 18"), 2017. This patch introduced the Iokath storyline, with daily missions, and the world boss tied to the "Gods From the Machine" Operation. It also brought back companions, improved the galaxy map interface, and expanded Master Mode Uprisings.[[283]](#cite_note-Update_5.2-283)

#### Game Update 5.3: Sisters of Carnage

**Game Update 5.3: Sisters of Carnage** was released on [July 11](/wiki/July_11 "July 11"), 2017. This patch centered on the new Aivela and Esne boss to the "Gods From the Machine" Operation and the new Manaan Stronghold on the ocean planet Manaan.[[284]](#cite_note-Update_5.3-284)

#### Game Update 5.4: Crisis on Umbara

**Game Update 5.4: Crisis on Umbara** was released on [August 22](/wiki/August_22 "August 22"), 2017. The update added the "Crisis on Umbara" flashpoint—a dramatic assault aboard a train on the planet [Umbara](/wiki/Umbara/Legends "Umbara/Legends") and introduced the Umbara Mobile Base stronghold, a customizable moving train. Ranked PvP Season 9 also began, and players gained new customization options for companion Senya Tirall.[[285]](#cite_note-Update_5.4-285)

#### Game Update 5.5: United Forces Preparation

**Game Update 5.5: United Forces Preparation** was released on [October 10](/wiki/October_10 "October 10"), 2017. The patch improved the Cartel Market interface.[[286]](#cite_note-Update_5.5-286) Game Update 5.5.1 expanded free-to-play, preferred, and subscriber character slots per server, reset all Legacy Family Trees, and a Legacy Storage Overflow for excess items.[[287]](#cite_note-Update_5.5.1-287)

#### Game Update 5.6: A Traitor Among the Chiss

**Game Update 5.6: A Traitor Among the Chiss** was released on [November 28](/wiki/November_28 "November 28"), 2017 and added a new Flashpoint on the planet [Copero](/wiki/Copero/Legends "Copero/Legends"), featuring the [Chiss Ascendacy](/wiki/Chiss_Ascendancy/Legends "Chiss Ascendancy/Legends") and continuing the traitor storyline introduced in earlier updates. The patch introduced new augment crafting tiers, improved Command Crate rewards, and allowed players to deposit credits into the Legacy Bank.[[288]](#cite_note-Update_5.6-288)

#### Game Update 5.7: Legacy of the Creators

**Game Update 5.7: Legacy of the Creators** was released on [January 23](/wiki/January_23 "January 23"), [2018](/wiki/2018 "2018") and introduced returning companions depending on player decisions, class balance changes, new gear tiers, and Command system adjustments were included to support both PvE and PvP playstyles.[[289]](#cite_note-Update_5.7-289)

#### Game Update 5.8: Command Authority

**Game Update 5.8: Command Authority** was released on [March 20](/wiki/March_20 "March 20"), 2018 and introduced a finale to the "Gods From the Machine" storyline with the addition of the new Operation boss [Izax](/wiki/Izax "Izax"). Alongside this major fight, the update overhauled Conquest, offering a revamped interface, expanded guild objectives, and enhanced rewards for guild-level participation. The update also introduced returning companions and a new companion romance.[[290]](#cite_note-Update_5.8-290)

#### Game Update 5.9: The Nathema Conspiracy

**Game Update 5.9: The Nathema Conspiracy** was released on [May 3](/wiki/May_3 "May 3"), 2018 and delivered a long-awaited conclusion to traitor storyline with a story-driven flashpoint set on [Nathema](/wiki/Nathema "Nathema") as players face a deadly enemy determined to obliterate the entire Alliance. The patch also introduced returning companions.[[291]](#cite_note-Update_5.9-291) Game Update 5.9.1 brought back the Nar Shaddaa Nightlife event alongside a week-long double‑rewards campaign for XP and Command XP.[[292]](#cite_note-Update_5.9.1-292) Game Update 5.9.2 introduced the [Rishi Hideout](/wiki/Rishi_Hideout "Rishi Hideout") stronghold and added the Mandalorian Battle Ring arena, revamped Warzone and matchmaking systems.[[293]](#cite_note-Update_5.9.2-293) Game Update 5.9.3 kicked off the Vandin Huttball event on the Sky Shredder map on [Vandin](/wiki/Vandin "Vandin").[[294]](#cite_note-Update_5.9.3-294)

#### Game Update 5.10: Jedi Under Siege

**Game Update 5.10: Jedi Under Siege** was released on [December 10](/wiki/December_10 "December 10"), 2018 and served as a final major patch to the *Knights of the Eternal Throne* expansion, continued the storyline to the planet Ossus. The patch also introduced Master Mode for the "Gods from the Machine" Operation, enhanced guild systems with a new interface and reduced flagship price, and expanded PvP capabilities with the introduction of custom matches.[[295]](#cite_note-Update_5.10-295) Game Update 5.10.1 introduced Geonosian Queen Lair Boss on Ossus.[[296]](#cite_note-Update_5.10.1-296) Game Update 5.10.2 focused on quality-of-life improvements. The patch introduced Guild Heraldry—customizable emblems for guild identity displayed across various in-game interfaces and completely overhauled the item/mount preview window.[[297]](#cite_note-Update_5.10.2-297) Game Update 5.10.3 introduced a recurring two-week "Pirate Incursion" event on Dantooine, featuring new daily and heroic missions, and enhanced planetary arrival cinematics.[[298]](#cite_note-Update_5.10.3-298)

#### Game Update 6.0: Onslaught

**Game Update 6.0: Onslaught** was released on [October 22](/wiki/October_22 "October 22"), [2019](/wiki/2019 "2019"), raising the level cap from 70 to 75. The update introduced two new planets—[Onderon](/wiki/Onderon/Legends "Onderon/Legends") and [Mek-Sha](/wiki/Mek-Sha "Mek-Sha"), along with a Flashpoint on [Corellia](/wiki/Corellia/Legends "Corellia/Legends") and a new Operation on [Dxun](/wiki/Dxun/Legends "Dxun/Legends"). It launched the "Spoils of War" gear system, featuring Tactical items, set bonuses, and greatly improved gear progression. The patch also included [Nautolans](/wiki/Nautolan/Legends "Nautolan/Legends") as a new playable species for the player characters.[[299]](#cite_note-Update_6.0-299)

#### Game Update 6.1: Pinnacles of Power

**Game Update 6.1: Pinnacles of Power** was released on [February 13](/wiki/February_13 "February 13"), [2020](/wiki/2020 "2020") and expanded the *Onslaught* storyline with the addition of the [Alderaan Noble Estate](/wiki/Alderaan_Noble_Estate "Alderaan Noble Estate") stronghold.[[300]](#cite_note-Update_6.1-300) Game Update 6.1.2 introduced the [All Worlds Ultimate Swoop Rally](/wiki/All_Worlds_Ultimate_Swoop_Rally "All Worlds Ultimate Swoop Rally")—a galaxy-wide racing event. It also launched Master Mode for the "Nature of Progress" Operation.[[301]](#cite_note-Update_6.1.2-301) Game Update 6.1.4 introduced the [Feast of Prosperity](/wiki/Feast_of_Prosperity/Legends "Feast of Prosperity/Legends") event.[[302]](#cite_note-Update_6.1.4-302)

#### Game Update 6.2: Echoes of Vengeance

**Game Update 6.2: Echoes of Vengeance** was released on [December 9](/wiki/December_9 "December 9"), 2020 and furthered the *Onslaught* storyline with new story content titled "Echoes of Oblivion," involving [Satele Shan](/wiki/Satele_Shan "Satele Shan")'s missing ship and the [Servants](/wiki/Servant "Servant") of the former Sith Emperor. The patch introduced a new Flashpoint—"Spirit of Vengeance" featuring [Mandalorian antagonists](/wiki/Hidden_Chain "Hidden Chain") stealing relics from [Shae Vizla's flagship](/wiki/Spirit_of_Vengeance_II "Spirit of Vengeance II"). Additional content included a new weekly login rewards system, UI enhancements like the Emote Window.[[303]](#cite_note-Update_6.2-303)

#### Game Update 6.3: The Dark Descent

**Game Update 6.3: The Dark Descent** was released on [April 27](/wiki/April_27 "April 27"), [2021](/wiki/2021 "2021") and served as the final major chapter of the *Onslaught* expansion. The patch introduced a new Flashpoint—"Secrets of the Enclave," featuring Darth Malgus on Dantooine. The update also debuted the Galactic Seasons system—titled "The Stranger from Kubindi"—a battlepass-like progression track with cosmetics, mounts, and a new companion as rewards through daily and weekly objectives.[[304]](#cite_note-Update_6.3-304)

#### Game Update 7.0: Legacy of the Sith

**Game Update 7.0: Legacy of the Sith** was released on [February 15](/wiki/February_15 "February 15"), [2022](/wiki/2022 "2022") and served as the new digital expansion for *The Old Republic*, raising the level cap from 75 to 80. It returned players to Manaan and introduced a thrilling new flashpoint on Elom. This patch brought new gameplay improvements—Combat Styles replaced the advanced class system. Subscribers could equip two Combat Styles per character, managed easily through the new loadout system. A revamped interface—including a modern character menu with tabs for combat styles and gear-boosted usability and the new character creation interface. The patch also launched the second season of Galactic Seasons—"Shadows of the Underworld,"[[305]](#cite_note-Update_7.0-305) with a new reputation track titled "The Shadow Syndicate," an underworld syndicate led by the Season 2 companion reward, [Fen Zeil](/wiki/Fen_Zeil "Fen Zeil").[[306]](#cite_note-Galactic_Season_2-306)

#### Game Update 7.1: Digging Deeper

**Game Update 7.1: Digging Deeper** was released on [August 2](/wiki/August_2 "August 2"), 2022 and continued the *Legacy of the Sith* storyline. Players returned to Elom to uncover Darth Malgus's fascination with [Darth Nul](/wiki/Darth_Nul "Darth Nul") and learn the fate of Padawan [Sa'har Kateen](/wiki/Sa%27har_Kateen "Sa'har Kateen"). The update included the new R‑4 Anomaly Operation, a challenging eight-player raid introducing veteran‑mode gear up to Item Rating 340. It also added a Manaan Daily Area featuring faction-specific storylines, daily and weekly missions, reputation tracks, achievements, and stronghold decorations. The patch also balanced the Combat Styles for classes, four new Tactical items available at the Supplies vendor.[[59]](#cite_note-Update_7.1-59)

#### Game Update 7.2: Showdown on Ruhnuk

**Game Update 7.2: Showdown on Ruhnuk** was released on [December 13](/wiki/December_13 "December 13"), 2022 and expanded the *Legacy of the Sith* storyline with a brand new planet—[Ruhnuk](/wiki/Ruhnuk "Ruhnuk"). Players follow [Shae Vizla](/wiki/Mandalore_the_Avenger "Mandalore the Avenger") and the Alliance Commander to confront [Heta Kol](/wiki/Heta_Kol "Heta Kol") and the Hidden Chain with a daily area, daily and weekly missions, achievements, and a reputation track. The update also reworked PvP—removing ranked queues in favor of a new Seasons system with 4v4 and 8v8 arenas, introduced interface improvements—Welcome Window, revamped minimap, new Deconstruct and Delete window, more utility bar customizations, and colorblind mode.[[307]](#cite_note-Update_7.2-307)

#### Game Update 7.3: Old Wounds

**Game Update 7.3: Old Wounds** was released on [June 13](/wiki/June_13 "June 13"), [2023](/wiki/2023 "2023") and featured the "Shrine of Silence" Flashpoint on Voss and continued the *Legacy of the Sith* storyline. The update included a new daily area on Voss, with reputation tracks, achievements, alongside quality-of-life changes.[[61]](#cite_note-Update_7.3-61)

#### Game Update 7.4: Chains in the Dark

**Game Update 7.4: Chains in the Dark** was released on [December 5](/wiki/December_5 "December 5"), 2023 and continued the Hidden Chain storyline on Ord Mantell and [Kessan's Landing](/wiki/Kessan%27s_Landing "Kessan's Landing"). Players engage in a new daily area, with a new world boss named [FR3-D0M](/wiki/FR3-D0M "FR3-D0M"), uncovered story secrets, and participated in "Chains in the Dark" quests. This patch also included cinematic lighting overhaul to all cutscenes and a completely revamped Galactic Trade Network, making it more accessible but also familiar to players, with a new advanced search section, and a more streamlined flow for claiming and selling items.[[63]](#cite_note-Update_7.4-63)

#### Game Update 7.5: Desperate Defiance

**Game Update 7.5: Desperate Defiance** was released on [May 29](/wiki/May_29 "May 29"), [2024](/wiki/2024 "2024") and continued the Hidden Chain storyline and expanded the game's content with new areas and features. Players explore the newly modernized on Nal Hutta, including the addition of the [Minboosa District](/wiki/Minboosa_District "Minboosa District"), a territory controlled by the crime lord [Vobbara Yusinduu](/wiki/Vobbara_Yusinduu "Vobbara Yusinduu"). The update introduced the Basilisk Prototype venture—adding [B3-S1](/wiki/B3-S1 "B3-S1") as a companion and a new [Dantooine Spring Abundance Festival](/wiki/Dantooine_Spring_Abundance_Festival "Dantooine Spring Abundance Festival") event to Dantooine with the addition of a new non-combat zone area—[Blba Groves](/wiki/Blba_Groves "Blba Groves"). It also launched PvP Season 6—"Great Pirate Hunt."[[308]](#cite_note-Update_7.5-308)

#### Game Update 7.6: Galactic Threads

**Game Update 7.6: Galactic Threads** was released on December 10, 2024. This patch introduced Dynamic Encounters and added character modernization enhancements. This patch brought art modernizations to Korriban, Tython, Hoth, and Ilum. A new lair boss—[Propagator Core XR-53](/wiki/XR-53 "XR-53") and the launch of PvP Season 7—"Path to Mastery" also launched with this update. This patch included no story content.[[309]](#cite_note-Update_7.6-309)

#### Game Update 7.7: Dynamic Worlds

**Game Update 7.7: Dynamic Worlds** was released on [May 28](/wiki/May_28 "May 28"), [2025](/wiki/2025 "2025"). It expanded Dynamic Encounters to new planet types—capital worlds, starter planets, and Ilum. It also introduced Master Mode for the XR‑53 "Relentless Replication" boss, a new Eras window for narrative timeline tracking, improved mission log interface, and PvP Season 8 "Champions of the Wild." This patch included no story content.[[310]](#cite_note-Update_7.7-310) Game Update 7.7.1 introduces Galactic Season 9 "Flashpoint Resurgence," improvements to Activity Finder, several quality-of-life changes of free-to-play and preferred players, and gears under level 80 no longer require Artifact Authorization. The character select screen has also been visually updated, now featuring improved lighting and a depth of field effect that better highlights the player character.[[311]](#cite_note-Update_7.7.1-311)

#### Game Update 7.8: Pursuit of Ruin

**Game Update 7.8: Pursuit of Ruin** was released on December 9, 2025. It released the *Galactic Threads* storyline with English voices, with French and German versions in progress. Players can participate in dynamic encounters on Dantooine in [a new area](/wiki/Jannimak_crash_site "Jannimak crash site") for level 80 players. PvP Season 9 "Gladiators of the Outer Rim" is released with new rewards including titles, achievements, flairs, armors, and a jetpack mount.[[312]](#cite_note-Update_7.8-312) Game Update 7.8.1 will be released before Spring [2026](/wiki/2026 "2026") and will release the *Master's Enigma* storyline and the tenth season of the Galactic Seasons.[[21]](#cite_note-Q4_2025-21)

#### Game Update 7.9: Legacy Reborn

**Game Update 7.9: Legacy Reborn** is set for release in Spring 2026 and will mark the final chapter of *Legacy of the Sith*. The update will introduce the tenth season of the PvP Season, while Game Update 7.9.1 will release the eleventh season of the Galactic Seasons.[[21]](#cite_note-Q4_2025-21)

### World Events

#### Rakghoul Outbreak

 [![Rakghoul Outbreak](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/Rakghoul_outbreak.png/revision/latest?cb=20231228224916) [![Rakghoul Outbreak](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/Rakghoul_outbreak.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20231228224916)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/Rakghoul_outbreak.png/revision/latest?cb=20231228224916) 

Rakghoul Outbreak

 

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Rakghoul pandemic](/wiki/Rakghoul_pandemic "Rakghoul pandemic")

:   "*Attention Republic citizens. The Health and Safety Council has updated its recommendations for dealing with extreme cases of rakghoul plague. Anyone who has suffered a full-body genetic mutation from rakghoul plague is now considered a high-risk threat to anyone nearby. As there is no cure for this disease once genetic mutation is complete, citizens are advised to employ lethal force to prevent further infections. If you are unable or unwilling to use lethal force, please contact Republic Military representatives. They will assist you.*"
:   ―Republic news reporter[[313]](#cite_note-YT-313)

The game's first World Event, **Rakghoul Outbreak**, began on [April 15](/wiki/April_15 "April 15"), 2012. Centered on Tatooine, the event introduced a number of limited time missions that dealt with the outbreak of the rakghoul plague on the planet, and locales such as Mos Ila and Anchorhead received environmental changes such as debris from the infected cruiser *Stardream* and special containment soldiers. The *Stardream* itself could be found in the northeastern corner of the Dune Sea region, and Codex entries revealed the history of the crash and also linked the event's origins with the recently released Operation Lost Island. Players earned special commendations for completing the daily missions, and the commendations could be spent at special vendors to purchase items that included new green-black color crystals, a Rakling pet, and rakghoul-styled customizations for companion characters. Players could also be infected with the rakghoul plague, and would die from the illness if not treated.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

On [April 20](/wiki/April_20 "April 20"), five days into the event, BioWare released the in-game news report by the [Republic News Network](/wiki/Republic_News_Network "Republic News Network") as a promotional video. The video gave an overview of the threat the rakghoul plague posed to the galaxy, and the news report ends when a bystander succumbs to the plague and is shot by Republic Military personnel. The event came to an end on [April 24](/wiki/April_24 "April 24"),[[314]](#cite_note-Outbreak_Video-314) and the missions, the *Stardream* and other event-related game features were removed at that time. However, the vendors for the event commendations remained in place to allow players to still redeem those commendations that they had not yet spent.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

#### The Grand Acquisitions Race

 [![The Grand Acquisitions Race](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/Grand_Acquisitions_Race.png/revision/latest?cb=20130427004133) [![The Grand Acquisitions Race](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/Grand_Acquisitions_Race.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20130427004133)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/38/Grand_Acquisitions_Race.png/revision/latest?cb=20130427004133) 

The Grand Acquisitions Race

 

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Grand Acquisitions Race](/wiki/Grand_Acquisitions_Race "Grand Acquisitions Race")

:   "*Recently, Chevin slaves and emissaries have been seen contacting mercenaries, scavengers and other underworld figures. All Imperial citizens are urged to—*"  
    "*Greetings from the Chevin Conglomerate. Our eternal purpose: to provide personal enrichment opportunities. All other claims are libelous. The Grand Acquisitions Race has begun. Profit opportunities are extensive for individuals capable of interstellar travel. Others need not apply.*"
:   ―The Chevin Conglomerate interrupts an Imperial News Network broadcast[[9]](#cite_note-Manual-9)

BioWare launched the game's second World Event, **The Grand Acquisitions Race** on [August 14](/wiki/August_14 "August 14"), 2012.[[315]](#cite_note-event2start-315) For the second event, BioWare preceded launch with the debut of the [Imperial News Network](/wiki/Imperial_News_Network_(Sith_Empire) "Imperial News Network (Sith Empire)") in-game report.[[316]](#cite_note-Acquisitions_Trailer-316) The event's story ties into the overall story arc involving the Gree species, with the mysterious [Chevin Conglomerate](/wiki/Chevin_Conglomerate "Chevin Conglomerate") of [Vinsoth](/wiki/Vinsoth/Legends "Vinsoth/Legends") announcing a galaxy-wide quest for artifacts so that they can appease the coming Gree fleet. In-game, their search manifested as a scavenger hunt for event-specific items in exchange for reward tokens which could be used to buy new items. The search involved nine artifacts, many of which could be found on Nar Shaddaa, while other artifacts were located on neutral worlds or each factions' capital. The event concluded on [August 21](/wiki/August_21 "August 21"), 2012.[[317]](#cite_note-event2end-317)

#### Relics of the Gree

 [![Relics of the Gree](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/Relics_of_the_Gree.png/revision/latest?cb=20130427005738) [![Relics of the Gree](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/Relics_of_the_Gree.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20130427005738)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/63/Relics_of_the_Gree.png/revision/latest?cb=20130427005738) 

Relics of the Gree

 

:   "*Elation progresses throughout the Enclave:* Gray Secant*, an ancient starship crafted by revered Gree ancestors, has reappeared from its multi-millennial task of exploration!* Gray Secant *has chosen the world you call Ilum for its next site of analysis. The intricacies of your culture's warfare dominate its interest. The Enclave deems you essential for analysis by* Gray Secant*. Join us on Ilum! Demonstrate combativeness for* Gray Secant*, and Gree technologies will be given in return!*"
:   ―A Gree transmission[[9]](#cite_note-Manual-9)

*The Old Republic*'s third World Event, **Relics of the Gree**, was announced on January 11, and it is a sequel to the events of the Grand Acquisitions Race.[[235]](#cite_note-Update_1.7_Announcement-235) Relics of the Gree is a recurring event that initially ran from February 12 through [February 26](/wiki/February_26 "February 26"), and it focuses on the arrival of the Gree starship known as the *[Gray Secant](/wiki/Gray_Secant "Gray Secant")* on the Western Ice Shelf. The Western Ice Shelf was redone as part of the event, and a number of new Gree-themed daily missions were added to the region as part of the event. Players who participated in the event and completed the daily missions earned Reputation with the Gree Enclave as part of Update 1.7's new Reputation system, and players with high enough Reputation could purchase exclusive gear from vendors who remained on Ilum even after the event ended.[[318]](#cite_note-Developer_Blog:_Relics_of_the_Gree-318) As a recurring event, Relics of the Gree returned to the game between March 12 and [March 26](/wiki/March_26 "March 26") as part of *The Old Republic*'s "March to Makeb" promotional campaign,[[319]](#cite_note-Double_XP-319) and was brought back May 21 through [May 28](/wiki/May_28 "May 28")[[320]](#cite_note-Relics_May-320) and [July 23](/wiki/July_23 "July 23") through August 6.[[321]](#cite_note-Relics_July-321) The World Event also returned between [December 17](/wiki/December_17 "December 17") to [January 1](/wiki/January_1 "January 1"), 2014,[[322]](#cite_note-Grinch-322) between [July 22](/wiki/July_22 "July 22") and [July 29](/wiki/July_29 "July 29"),[[323]](#cite_note-Event_Page-323) and [February 24](/wiki/February_24 "February 24") to [March 3](/wiki/March_3 "March 3").[[324]](#cite_note-Relics_Feb-March-324)

#### Bounty Contract Week

 [![Bounty Contract Week](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/Bounty_Contract_Week.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130820155330) [![Bounty Contract Week](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/Bounty_Contract_Week.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20130820155330)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/Bounty_Contract_Week.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130820155330) 

Bounty Contract Week

 

:   "*Got blasters? Get credits!*"
:   ―The Bounty Brokers Association[[325]](#cite_note-Bounty_Contract-325)

**Bounty Contract Week** is a monthly event that was introduced with Game Update 2.3 and lasts an entire week. First announced on July 5, Bounty Contract Week is centered in the new Cartel Bazaar sections of the faction fleets, and is presented in-universe as a list of contracts posted by the Bounty Brokers Association in the Bazaar for targets across the galaxy. The contracts outlines information on the target, contact information for the client, and underworld contacts who can aid players, and the targets are chosen from criminal elements and other law-breaking individuals. High-profile targets are designated as "Kingpins" and can be hunted through Kingpin Contracts, authorization for which can be purchased in exchange for five completed bounty contracts. Every day, a player may sign up for one standard and one Kingpin contract, and the contract's completion requires the target's death or capture—but players will also be rated on their resource-handling aptitude and their investigative skills. Contracts are available at Level 15, and each contract will scale its difficulty and rewards to the player's level.[[249]](#cite_note-Bounty_Contract_Week-249) The first Bounty Contract Week began on August 14 and continued for seven days,[[247]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Update_2.3-247) and the second occurrence of the event ran from September 10 through [September 17](/wiki/September_17 "September 17").[[326]](#cite_note-Bounty_Contract_September-326) Thus far, the event has returned each month since except for January 2014, and lasts a week each time.[[327]](#cite_note-Bounty_December-327)

#### Life Day

 [![Life Day](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/TOR_Life_Day_Event.png/revision/latest?cb=20131220190752) [![Life Day](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/TOR_Life_Day_Event.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20131220190752)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/TOR_Life_Day_Event.png/revision/latest?cb=20131220190752) 

Life Day

 

:   "*It has come to the Empire's attention that dissident elements engaging in a tawdry and potentially dangerous seasonal event are planning to infect Imperial space with their insipid notions. This so-called 'Life Day' encourages activities unbecoming of an Imperial citizen, including but not limited to:*

    :   *Dancing in inclement weather*
    :   *Singing unpatriotic carols*
    :   *Nonviolent physical contact with Wookiees*
:   *This disgraceful menace of a 'holiday', during which time you are expected to comply fully with this edict, will last approximately two weeks on the Galactic Standard Calendar.*"
:   ―Imperial Edict GR-1NC4[[328]](#cite_note-Imperial_Edict-328)

The Wookiee holiday of Life Day, an event previously celebrated in *Star Wars Galaxies* around Christmas, was celebrated briefly in *Star Wars: The Old Republic* around Christmas 2012. In 2013, however, a larger **Life Day** event was launched where the [Master of Ceremonies](/wiki/Master_of_Ceremonies "Master of Ceremonies") sold holiday-themed items on both factions' fleets, and an activity involving "Life Day snowball bombs" was available. The snowballs were thrown at other players in hopes of gaining "Snow-Covered Parcels" from doing so; the parcels were used as currency with the Master of Ceremonies and could unlock items such as unique vehicles and titles. The day before the event, an [Imperial Edict GR-1NC4](/wiki/Imperial_Edict_GR-1NC4 "Imperial Edict GR-1NC4") was posted on the game's official site decrying the activities of the Master of Ceremonies and warning all Imperial citizens to report such activities. The event ran from December 17 to January 1, 2014,[[322]](#cite_note-Grinch-322) and returned the following holiday season between [December 16](/wiki/December_16 "December 16") and [January 6](/wiki/January_6 "January 6"), [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015") with new Parcel Droids that would potentially reward players with Stronghold decorations when hit with snowball bombs.[[329]](#cite_note-Life_Day_2014-329)

#### Rakghoul Resurgence

 [![Rakghoul Resurgence](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/Rakghoul_Resurgence.png/revision/latest?cb=20140124001103) [![Rakghoul Resurgence](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/Rakghoul_Resurgence.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20140124001103)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/Rakghoul_Resurgence.png/revision/latest?cb=20140124001103) 

Rakghoul Resurgence

 

:   "*The Hyland Organization for Rakghoul Neutralization (T.H.O.R.N.) has issued an official level-2 emergency alert concerning an outbreak of the Rakghoul plague on Alderaan. Wide-spread infections have been reported near both House Organa and House Thul, while scattered reports of infection traceable to Alderaan are now flooding in from across the galaxy. Quarantines have been put in place to restrict traffic of the plague off-world, but exceptions will be made for individuals with priority clearance.*"
:   ―An emergency alert concerning Alderaan[[330]](#cite_note-Emergency_Alert-330)

The **Rakghoul Resurgence** World Event was first hinted at in the Achievement system, which included entries for the upcoming event; the event first went live on January 21, 2014. Lasting until [January 28](/wiki/January_28 "January 28"), the event occurs on the planet Alderaan, where the rakghoul plague has resurfaced, and is accessible by players who are Level 25 or higher. Most of the event takes place in the Rakghoul Tunnels map, which are a set of Killik tunnels underneath King's Pass in which a nest of rakghouls have been discovered. The tunnels are accessed via [the Spike](/wiki/The_Spike_(weapon) "The Spike (weapon)"), a massive mining tower that has breached the tunnels, and players assist the operatives of T.H.O.R.N. in battling the rakghouls and containing the outbreak through a number of daily missions. A powerful Operation boss, the [Eyeless](/wiki/Eyeless "Eyeless"), is available to battle during the event.[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24) A recurring event, Rakghoul Resurgence was planned to appear on Tatooine, Quesh, and Corellia in future installments.[[323]](#cite_note-Event_Page-323) On June 10, Associate Producer [Andrew Horwitz](/wiki/Andrew_Horwitz "Andrew Horwitz") stated that the Rakghoul Resurgence event would not return that summer,[[259]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_Update_2.8-259) but the event arrived on Tatooine between [August 5](/wiki/August_5 "August 5") and [August 12](/wiki/August_12 "August 12") despite Horwitz's statement, and later returned again on Corellia between [October 28](/wiki/October_28 "October 28") and [November 4](/wiki/November_4 "November 4").[[24]](#cite_note-TOR-24)

#### Nar Shaddaa Nightlife

 [![Nar Shaddaa Nightlife](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/Soovada.png/revision/latest?cb=20150808133127) [![Nar Shaddaa Nightlife](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/Soovada.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20150808133127)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8f/Soovada.png/revision/latest?cb=20150808133127) 

Nar Shaddaa Nightlife

 

:   "*On the Republic and Imperial fleets, you will notice some new floating advertisement terminals perhaps too enticing to ignore. When activated, you are a captive audience for the Star Cluster and Club Vertica Casino advertisements, inviting you to come and experience the Nar Shaddaa Nightlife for a limited time. The heart of Nar Shaddaa Nightlife is the Smuggler's Luck and Kingpin's Bounty slot machines. Through these machines, players can win unique weapons, armor, cosmetic abilities, and mounts including an exclusive Rancor mount!*"
:   ―Chris Schmidt[[263]](#cite_note-Developer_Update:_Spoils_of_War-263)

The **Nar Shaddaa Nightlife** World Event, originally promoted as the **Festival of Splendor** World Event, was introduced with Game Update 2.8: Spoils of War and corresponds to the annual Hutt celebration of *[Soovada](/wiki/Soovada "Soovada")*, or "Splenderous Summer," on Nar Shaddaa. It features expanded functionalities for the Club Vertica and Star Cluster casinos, introducing slot machines and tokens with a variety of rewards. Players could use the casinos' slot machine to play either "Smuggler's Luck" or "Kingpin's Bounty;" the games reward players with Golden Certificates that could then be redeemed for exclusive items.[[262]](#cite_note-Game_Update_2.8:_Spoils_of_War-262)

#### All Worlds Ultimate Swoop Rally

 [![All Worlds Ultimate Swoop Rally](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/TheAllWorldsUltimateSwoop.png/revision/latest?cb=20201117172008) [![All Worlds Ultimate Swoop Rally](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/TheAllWorldsUltimateSwoop.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20201117172008)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/TheAllWorldsUltimateSwoop.png/revision/latest?cb=20201117172008) 

All Worlds Ultimate Swoop Rally

 

Introduced with Game Update 6.1.2, the **All Worlds Ultimate Swoop Rally** is a recurring, [swoop racing](/wiki/Swoop_racing/Legends "Swoop racing/Legends") event across multiple planets—Dantooine, Tatooine, and Onderon. Players choose from three swoop gangs—[Horizon's Razor](/wiki/Horizon%27s_Razor "Horizon's Razor"), [Pit Screamers](/wiki/Pit_Screamers "Pit Screamers"), and [Blatant Beks](/wiki/Blatant_Beks "Blatant Beks")—each offering daily challenge missions tailored to their style. Rewards include exclusive items—gold and regular swoop mounts, outfits, droid mini-pets, stronghold decorations, and titles.[[331]](#cite_note-All_Worlds_Ultimate_Swoop_Rally-331)

#### Feast of Prosperity

 [![Feast of Prosperity](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/FeastProsperityOnslaught.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201011182524) [![Feast of Prosperity](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/FeastProsperityOnslaught.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20201011182524)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/FeastProsperityOnslaught.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201011182524) 

Feast of Prosperity

 

The **Feast of Prosperity** is a recurring celebration held annually in the late fall introduced in Game Update 6.1.4. The event is hosted by two rising Hutt nobles, [Gaboorga](/wiki/Gaboorga "Gaboorga") the Abundant and [Duuba](/wiki/Duuba "Duuba") the Magnanimous. This event focuses on cooking minigames, delivering food to guests, and collecting special ingredients from around the galaxy[[332]](#cite_note-Feast_of_Prosperity-332). By completing daily and weekly tasks, players earn tokens that can be used to get rewards such as outfits, weapons, mounts, pets, and stronghold decorations.[[333]](#cite_note-Prepare-333)

#### Dantooine Spring Abundance Festival

 [![Dantooine Spring Abundance Festival](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5b/LotS-DantooineSpringEvent.png/revision/latest?cb=20240630065733) [![Dantooine Spring Abundance Festival](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5b/LotS-DantooineSpringEvent.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20240630065733)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5b/LotS-DantooineSpringEvent.png/revision/latest?cb=20240630065733) 

Dantooine Spring Abundance Festival

 

The **Dantooine Spring Abundance Festival** was introduced in Game Update 7.5: *Desperate Defiance* released on [2024](/wiki/2024 "2024"). This recurring festival is centered around social activities and offers players a break from combat-focused gameplay by engaging in relaxing, farm-themed activities. Players can participate in the event from the Fleet and travel to [Blba Groves](/wiki/Blba_Groves "Blba Groves"), a secondary landing zone on Dantooine. Players can engage in various daily and weekly missions. Completing the missions earns players Farmland Medals, which can be exchanged for a variety of exclusive rewards at the Token Vendor.[[334]](#cite_note-Dantooine_Spring_Abundance_Festival-334)

### Digital Expansions

#### *Rise of the Hutt Cartel*

 [![Rise of the Hutt Cartel](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/Rise_of_the_Hutt_Cartel_TOR.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20121218173132) [![Rise of the Hutt Cartel](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/Rise_of_the_Hutt_Cartel_TOR.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121218173132)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0e/Rise_of_the_Hutt_Cartel_TOR.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20121218173132) 

*Rise of the Hutt Cartel*

 

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Star Wars: The Old Republic: Rise of the Hutt Cartel](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Old_Republic:_Rise_of_the_Hutt_Cartel "Star Wars: The Old Republic: Rise of the Hutt Cartel")

:   "*The Hutts will not be allowed to expand their dominion at our expense.*"
:   ―Supreme Chancellor Leontyne Saresh[[11]](#cite_note-ROTHC-11)

The game's first Digital Expansion, ***Rise of the Hutt Cartel***, was first announced on December 18, 2012, with an intended release in the spring of 2013. *Rise of the Hutt Cartel* introduces a new dual-faction planet, Makeb, upon which the players battle the forces of the Hutt Cartel as the organization attempts to become a third galactic power. The expansion also increases the level cap to Level 55, and is offered for a regular price of $19.99, though subscribes were initially able to pre-order the game for only $9.99.[[335]](#cite_note-Hutt_Cartel_Press-335) On [January 23](/wiki/January_23 "January 23"), it was announced that players who preorder the expansion would receive three exclusive in-game items: a holostatue of the Hutt Dr. Juvard Illip Oggurobb, a [Makrin Seedling](/wiki/Makrin_creeper "Makrin creeper") Mini-Pet, and the "Scourge of the Hutts" title.[[336]](#cite_note-Rise_Cartel_Exclusive-336)

Further Developer Blogs, Updates, and trailers in March gave further information on Makeb and its history,[[337]](#cite_note-Developer_Update:_Overview_of_Makeb-337) and on [March 12](/wiki/March_12 "March 12") *The Old Republic* announced Double XP weekends as part of their "March to Makeb" promotion. During the final three weekends of March and the first weekend of April, players were able to gain double the amount of experience so that they could reach Level 50 in time for the release of *Rise of the Hutt Cartel*, and the Relics of the Gree event was re-released to further entice players.[[319]](#cite_note-Double_XP-319) Finally, on [March 25](/wiki/March_25 "March 25"), BioWare and LucasArts announced a release date of [April 14](/wiki/April_14 "April 14") for *Rise of the Hutt Cartel*, and Game Update 2.0 was released on April 9 to accompany the opening of pre-order early access to the expansion.[[338]](#cite_note-Digital_Expansion_April-338) Starting September 12, 2013, *Rise of the Hutt Cartel* is now free for subscribers as a subscription benefit.[[200]](#cite_note-ROTHC_Free-200)
